Goblin Gliders 140 5 2 7 1 7 3 0.3 4 0.2
Goblin Midget Submarines 190 3 5 12 8 5 8 7 0.3 3 0.2
Special Units:
Hobgoblins (Armory, Cost 40) – A replacement unit of Halberdiers as 2nd tier polearm unit, Hobgoblins serve
secondary role as road builders as well as main line holder for goblin race with ability to budding clone of
themselves in combat.
Warbosses (Fighter’s Guild+War College, Cost 120) – Considered as commander unit among goblin, although
they have decent fighting capability and number, they don’t have any special fighting ability apart from buffing
To-Hit and To-Defend based on number of goblins in the army. Although they could not budding clone, they
have ability to regenerate after combat.
Spider Riders (Smithy+Stable, Cost 80) – Different from most of cavalry type units, Spider Riders don’t have
first strike. The role of this unit is mainly an economical version of Giant Spiders with major damage dealing
coming from poison and support other units with 1 charge of web. So, this unit serve more as support unit rather
than assault one.
Tricksters (Town Hall+Alchemist’s Guild, Cost 50) – The first of Goblin’s “wacky” units, Tricksters are an indirect
fighters with low melee strength but decent thrown, armor, ability to merge and movement of 3, the unit is
designed to hit and run. This unit also has the ability to install trap with fast 2 turns recharge, this allows
Tricksters to do indirect fight and harass the enemies.
Rabblerousers (Town Hall+Shrine, Cost 65) – This unit is a replacement for shaman as 1st tier cleric but that
could not use healing spell and also politicians instead of clerics. Instead, Rabblerousers have Resistance-for-All
+1 and ability to cast a few charges of Blaze of Glory so Rabblerousers are offensive cult leaders that turn
cultists into suicide attackers and mitigate effects of magic curses and poison.
Hexers (Sage’s Guild+Witches’ Convent, Cost 110) – This unit is a replacement for disciples as 1st tier spell
caster but losing casting skill but gain illusion attack and a few charges of Liability. Although individual figure’s
attack power is a bit lower than generic disciples in term of raw strength but higher in figures, illusion attack, and
poison ability make their total attack strength decent and prime for buffing.
Arsonists (Fighter’s Guild+Library, Cost 60) – This unit is a replacement for shieldbearers in their position in
roster but its fighting style is completely different. Instead of fast-moving shielded units, Arsonists are double
attackers of both fire breath and melee. This allows Arsonists to able to attack flying units. Main defensive perk
of Arsonists are causing fear among enemies by how crazy these pyromaniacs are.
Night Goblins (Fighter’s Guild+Miner’s Guild, Cost 90) – This is a replacement for crossbowmen as 2nd tier
physical range attacker but instead focus on attack power of crossbow, Night Goblins focus more on stealth
instead with majority of damage coming from poison attack.
Mechaniacs (Town Hall+University, Cost 90) – This is a replacement for engineers but does not have ability to
build road. Instead, Mechaniacs focus on their role as mechanical unit support with ability to construct field
catapult, buff other mechanical units, and heal mechanical units by 1 Health at the end of turn if their Health is
below 50%.
Poxbearers (Sage’s Guild+Witches’ Convent, Cost 180) – This is one of “wackier” units of Goblin race. Although
Poxbearers have decent attack power with secondary attack as Resistance-check attack, their main gimmick is
ability to spread plague to the enemy at the beginning of combat (powerful combat global debuff of -3 Attack, -3
Defend, -3 Resistance) at cost of cause minor debuff on their own side. Although its minor debuff on the same
side would be removed upon the death of this unit, great debuff on enemy side would go on until the end of
combat.
Doom Wheels (Fighter’s Guild+Mechanician’s Guild, Cost 140) – This unit is 2nd tier mechanical light cavalry
with very powerful offensive power and speed but paper thin defend with main defensive ability is causing fear
and large shield. One of the wackier functions of this unit is that once Health reduces lower than 50% the unit
would allowed to use its special red button that would trigger self-destruction and bring serious damage to
surrounding enemies and allies.
Gliders (Hangar+Alchemist’s Guild, Cost 180) – These fighter-bomber hang-gliders are only flying unit of the
Goblin and one of a few mechanical flying units in game. Flying by exploit wind from permanent Guardian Wind
enchantment, the gliders are fast moving with strength of attack coming from their bomb and their numbers but
almost no protection from anything else apart from small missile by permanent Guardian Wind enchantment.
Midget Submarines (Mechanician’s Guild+Shipyard, Cost 250) – This unit is the wackiest unit in Goblin roster.
Midget Submarines are small submerging craft armed with torpedoes and protection coming from immunities to
different kinds of attacks the unit gains upon submerging. Due to its attack and def need to be submerged,
Midget Submarines will not fly (even if have enchantment that grant them flying) in combat if possible. If the unit
fought combat overland, if the unit does not have enchantment that grant non-corporeal, the unit would not be
able to submerge in combat.
NEW RACE Hawkmen (Arcanus)
Tilted Towards Military Race
Characteristics: 40 growth, 0 outpost growth. +0.25max pop per mountain, +1/2 power per population
Special Building: Altar of the Sun (required mountain/hill/volcano)
Building limitations: Dock and Shipyard, Bank, Stables, City Wall, Fortification, Brewery, Hillfort, Warlord’s
Hold
Hawkmen is a new race introduced by Warlord mod.
Hawkmen are winged humanoid people living in mountainous region of Arcanus. Different from beastmen and
other half-animal people, they have 6 limbs. They have strong affinity with primal forces, this makes some
scholars consider Hawkmen to be mortal descendents of their heralds.
Hawkmen are spiritual but openminded people, this is the only race that could build both temple and cathedral.
Hawkmen economic potential is mainly limited to strategies that exploit religious buildings the most. Otherwise,
hawkmen could not build any economic buildings beyond basic marketplace and have the lowest fertility rate
among Arcanian races.
Their military is however formidable. It is the norm rather than exception for female hawkmen to participate in
combat. Flying combined with first strike is a great tactical combo and nearly all recruitable units are racial
uniques. Hawkmen higher tier units dominate with abilities and special traits as opposed to sheer might and
have the only recruitable unit with magic immunity.
Normal Units: First Strike, Flying, -1 Figure
Spearmen, Swordsmen
Generic Mechanical Units: Mountaineer
Catapult, Ballistarace unit cost Figures Melee throw/breath Range Ammo Armor Resist Health to hit Move Poison ToDefend

Hawkman Swordsmen 30 5 4 4 4 1 0.3 2 0.3
Hawkman Harpies 40 5 1 4 3 3 2 4 1 0.3 3 0.3
Hawkman Eagle Warrior 65 5 5 4 5 2 0.3 4 0.3
Hawkman Enchantress 80 3 3 3 6 2 0.3 2 3 0.3
Hawkman Tomahawks 120 5 5 5 6 3 0.3 3 0.3

Special Units:
Harpies (cost 40, mill) – A skirmishing unit with range attacks (3 ammo), decent mobility, and high thrown rating.
Eagle Warriors (cost 65, armory) – combine the traits of cavalry and halberdier while coming with +1 resistance.
Tomahawks (cost 120, fighter's guild) – These are more damaging and durable than Eagle Warriors, but with 1
lower movement point. The high damage potential combined with flying and first strike adds to unit's survivability,
although they are vulnerable to ranged attacks.
Enchantress (cost 80, sage guild) – Replacement of generic disciples. Althrough they don't use ranged attacks,
they can fight properly in melee with poison hex and could curse enemy to unnatural slumber (black sleep)
Sky Lantern (Mechanician Guild cost 100) – A 1-figure slow moving unit with good sight, ranged armor piercing
attacks, and thrown.
Sirens (cost 180, Wizard's Guild) – Supernaturally seductive lady (1 charge of possession) that bring unnatural
demise to any who oppose her (death gaze), thus they are particularly dangerous in close combat.
Holy Mothers (cost 330, Temple, Cathedral) – Worshipped as goddess on earth. They are excellent healers,
could bless allies with much higher resistance, windwalks the army, and have a supernatural immunity to magic.
They take prohibitive cost to recruit and they walk the path of non-violence with 0 attack rating, thus their
usefulness depends on the armies they support.
Huichilobos (cost 230, Armorer's Guild) - elite sacred warriors of Hawkmen society. Dressed as spirits of the sun
and armed with poisonous serpentine hooked sword and throwing weaponry. They are immune to fire and death
curse and could summon phantom warriors to aid them in battle.
Buildings:
There are new buildings added in Warlord mod. Each races have at least one unique buildings, usually tie to
terrain type. Raider races (Barbarian, Gnoll, Troll) gain a few more buildings to support their more warlike
activity. Some buildings are available to most of the races
Generic Economy Buildings:
NEW: Dock (150 Production, 0 Upkeep) requires to construct on coastal city. This building is split up from old
Shipyard/Dock and Shipyard. This part of the old building is for access to sea bounty included trade bonus and
food generation from each overland water tiles near city with 1 food generate per tile and 2 food for river mouth
tile. This building also allows city to build Trireme. Every race except Hawkman could build this building.
Marketplace (80 Production, 0 Upkeep) is a basic economy building. This building serves as a central hub of
commerce where additional taxes are easily collected. It produces an additional +7 Gold each turn. All races
could access to this building.
Bank (200 Production, 2 Upkeep) requires Marketplace and University to be constructed. This building
enhances a town's commercial operations, boosting Gold income from the city by 30%. Every race except
Barbarian, Gnoll, Troll, and Hawkman could build this building.
Merchant’s Guild (400 Production, 3 Upkeep) requires Bank and Shipyard, and need to be coastal city due to
Dock as requirement by extension, to be constructed. This building is a sophisticated and organized hub of
prosperity, increasing Gold income from the city by 40%! This building is only available to cities of Beastman,
Dark Elf, Draconian, Halfling, High Elf, High Man, Nomad, Orc, Xuanyuan, or Rakhshasa race.
Granary (80 Production, 0 Upkeep) is a basic food and growth building. This building functions as a storage
facility for the city's food surplus. It increases Maximum Population by 5 and generates 4 Food. Every race
except Nomad could build this building.
Farmer's Market (150 Production, 1 Upkeep) requires Granary and Marketplace to be constructed. This building
serves as a centralized hub for trading the city's food surplus. It accelerates Population Growth by 40 and
generates 1 Gold for every two Population Units. Every race except Nomad and Goblin could build this building.
Animist’s Guild (240 Production, 2 Upkeep) requires Granary and Forester's Guild, which means need forest
nearby at point of building Forester's Guild by extension but forest does not requires after Forester's Guild is
built, to be constructed. This building increases each Farmer's Food harvest by 2 and enhances the healing rate
of units inside the city by 66%. Every race except Goblin and Nomad could build this building.
Generic Research Buildings: These buildings generate Research points as main resource. Sage Master retort
reduces construction cost of buildings in this category by 15%.
Library (80 Production, 0 Upkeep) is a basic education and research building. This building serves as a
repository for knowledge and scholarship. It contributes +4 spell research points. All races could access to this
building. All races could access to this building.
University (160 Production, 1 Upkeep) requires Library, and Town Hall to be constructed. This building stands
as a bastion of education and scholarship. It contributes +6 spell Research points. This building is also serve as
key buildings to many of higher tier of economy and production related buildings too. Every races except Gnoll,
and Troll could access to this building.
Sage's Guild (400 Production, 2 Upkeep) requires University, and Alchemist’s Guild to be constructed. This
building is dedicated to the advanced study of magic and understanding the universe. It adds +12 spell
Research points. Progressing beyond this building tier requires the casting of Tree of Knowledge. Disciples units
and magician units of similar class usually required this building to recruit. Every race except Barbarian, Dwarf,
Gnoll, and Troll could access to this building.
Generic Magic Buildings:
Magic Market (100 Production, 0 Upkeep) requires Marketplace to be constructed. This building accommodates
novice mages practicing witchcraft and selling various talismans. It generates +4 magic Power. Every race
except Dwarf could build this building.
Wizard's Guild (800 Production, 3 Upkeep) requires Magic Market, and Sage’s Guild to be constructed. This
building serves as a hub for the study and practice of magic. It enhances magic power by +12 and increases
spell research points by +2. This building is also a requirement for recruitment of Magisters and magician units of
similar class. Every race except Barbarian, Dwarf, Gnoll, Goblin, and Troll could build this building after casting
Tree of Knowledge.
Monument (75 Production, 0 Upkeep) is basic casting skill boosting building. This building aids in channeling
magical power across distant lands. It enhances combat casting skill by adding +180 SP to a wizard's skill pool.
Every race except Dwarf, and Gnoll could build this building.
Linking Tower (500 Production, 4 upkeep) requires Monument, and Sage’s Guild to be constructed. This
building connects a city to ley lines, facilitating the channeling of magical power across vast distances. It
enhances combat casting skill by adding +1200 SP to a wizard's skill pool. Every race except Barbarian, Dwarf,
Gnoll, and Troll could build this building after casting Tree of Knowledge.
Amplifying Tower (900 Production, 7 upkeep) requires Alchemist’s Guild, and Sage’s Guild to be constructed.
This building tunes Aether to facilitate easier spellcasting, increasing Overland Casting Skill by +7. Every race
except Barbarian, Dwarf, Gnoll, and Troll could build this building after casting Tree of Knowledge.
Generic Religion Buildings:
Shrine (120 Production, 0 Upkeep) is a basic religious building. This building offers spiritual solace to the people
of the city. It increases Religious Power by +2 and reduces Unrest by 1 level. All races could access to this
building.
Monastery (200 Production, 1 Upkeep) requires Shrine, and Town Hall to be constructed. This building serves
as a central hub for the study and teaching of religion within the city. It adds +4 Religious Power and reduces
Unrest by 1. Every race except Barbarian, Gnoll, Goblin, Klackon, and Troll could build this building.
Cathedral (500 Production, 2 Upkeep) requires Monastery and Town Hall to be constructed. This building
represent monotheism and Tolkien’s freepeople races’ religion. It designates the city as the center of worship for
the one true divinity. Through its unified and focused faith, a cathedral adds 6 Religious Power and reduces
Unrest by 2. This building is only available to cities of Draconian, Dwarf, Halfling, High Elf, High Man, or
Hawkman race.
NEW: Temple (400 Production, 1 Upkeep) requires Monastery and Town Hall to be constructed. This building is
represent polytheism and an alternative upgrade of Cathedral for some races. It adds 4 religious Power and
reduces Unrest by 1. It also provides an extra 2 religious Power and reduces Unrest by 1 for each Nightshade,
Wild Game, and Orihalcon resource available in city’s vicinity. This building is only available to cities of
Beastman, Dark Elf, Lizardman, Nomad, Orc, Rakhshasa, or Hawkman race.
Oracle (360 Production, 2 Upkeep) requires Shrine and Town Hall to be constructed. This building offers the city
magical guidance, detecting all enemies within 4 squares and serve as religious building in reducing Unrest by 3.
Although this building considered as religious building, it does not generate religious Power. This building could
be augmented to generate +4 religious Power under influence of Ruler of Underworld global enchantment. All
races could access to this building. All races except Goblin could access to this building.
NEW: Witches’ Convent (400 Production, 3 Upkeep) requires Shrine and Magic Market to be constructed. This
building offers the city magical protections. It generates +4 religious Power, and may curse units that attack the
city with common and uncommon curses. Although this building is considered as religious building, it does not
offer Unrest reduction. This building is only available to cities of Barbarian, Gnoll, Orc, Troll, and Hawkman race.
Generic Production Buildings:
Smithy (75 Production, 0 Upkeep) is the basic building for city production and military. This building specializes
in developing and producing high-quality weaponry and tools, serving as a fundamental building in any town. It
generates 3 Production and is essential for producing most military units. Each outpost receives this building for
free at time of founding but it could be destroyed and rebuilt. All races could access to this building.
Mill (80 Production, 0 Upkeep) is a basic production building of the city. This building boosts production by
relieving farmers' workload, allowing for more productive activities. It increases base Production by 1, with an
additional +0.5 for each Farmer population in the city. All races could access to this building.
Town Hall (80 Production, 0 Upkeep) is a basic production and civic building of the city. This building serves as
the hub of city governance, enabling the construction of advanced knowledge buildings and generating 0.5
production per worker in the city. All races could access to this building.
Miner’s Guild (200 Production, 2 Upkeep) is a basic production building of the city. This building educates
workers in the intricacies of mining, boosting special mineral bonuses by +50% and production by +25%. Every
races except Lizardman could build this building.
Mechanician’s Guild (400 Production, 4 Upkeep) requires University and Miner’s Guild to be constructed. This
building imparts advanced engineering techniques and enhances the productivity of each worker. It increases
city production by 1.5 units of production per worker. Every races except Barbarian, Gnoll, Lizardman, Troll, and
Rakhshasa could build this building.
Generic Multi-functions Buildings:
Forester's Guild (130 Production, 1 Upkeep) requires Mill and presence of forest near the city to be
constructed. This building trains skilled hunters and lumberjacks, boosting Production by +10% and increasing
Food harvest by +4, with an additional +2 for each area of Wild Game in the city's vicinity. All races could access
to this building.
Alchemist’s Guild (150 Production, 2 Upkeep) requires Library to be constructed. This building equips all new
troops with magical weapons, increasing their chance To-Hit by +10%. It also enables the use of Mithril,
Nightshade, Adamantium, and Orihalcon in the production of troops. Nightshade counters or dispels hostile
spells targeting the city with a strength of 100, and enhances the effects of Temple. This building could be
augmented by Philosopher’s Stone city enchantment to generate 12 Gold. Every race except Barbarian could
build this building.
Coliseum (250 Production, 0 Upkeep) requires Barracks and Fighter’s Guild to be constructed. This building
entertains the population, reducing Unrest by 1 and increasing Fame by 5. Every races except Halfling, and
Klackon could build this building.
NEW: Brewery (200 Production, 2 Upkeep) requires Farmer’s Market and Town Hall to be constructed. This
building consumes food equal to 50% of population units in the city, and +25% if the city has a Dock, and
convert them into Gold at rate 3 gold per unit of food consume this way. This building is also reduce unrest in the
city by 1. This building is only available to cities of Barbarian, Dwarf, Gnoll, Goblin, or Troll race.
NEW: Warlord’s Hold (400 Production, 5 Upkeep) requires Town Hall and War College to be constructed. This
building reduces the cost to recruit new units from the city by 25% and doubles the strength of garrison units in
reducing Unrest (1 unit per -1 unrest compared to normally 2 units per -1 unrest). For Wizard who start the game
with Barbarian, Gnoll or Troll (so called ‘Raiders Races’) as starting race, This building grants garrison strength
of 12 units distribute among cities under wizard’s control that does not have Warlord’s Hold. This building is only
available to cities of Barbarian, Gnoll, Goblin, or Troll race.
Generic Military Buildings: They are generally 20-30% more expensive to build than in Caster of Magic but
their upkeep costs are cheaper. Warlord retort reduces construction cost of these buildings by 15%.
NEW: Armory (150 Production, 1 Upkeep) requires Smithy to be constructed and is a prerequisite for Barracks
and Fighter’s Guild. This building serves as gap between Smithy and Fighter’s Guild from Classic Master of
Magic is now coming back requirement for Halberdiers level units once again. All races could access to this
building.
Barracks (200 Production, 1 Upkeep) requires Armory to be constructed and is a prerequisite for Coliseum and
War College. This building enable a city to train and organize regular military units. Without barracks, a city can't
train regular military units. All units created in the town gain +1 Level. Every races except Halfling could build this
building.
War College (540 Production, 3 Upkeep) requires Barracks and Fighter’s Guild to be constructed. This building
functions as a hub for teaching battle strategy, tactics, and advanced fighting techniques. All new troops begin
as Veterans. This building is also serve as requirement replacement for elite units of raider races that could not
build Armorer’s Guild. Every races except Halfling could build this building.
Fighter's Guild (200 Production, 2 Upkeep) requires Armory to be constructed and is a prerequisite for
Coliseum, War College, Maritime Guild, Armorer’s Guild, and Fantastic Stable. This building trains soldiers and
unlocks superior unit types (Shieldbearers and their equivalents). Progressing beyond this building tier requires
casting the Tree of Knowledge spell. All races could access to this building.
Armorer's Guild (600 Production, 4 Upkeep) requires Smithy, and Fighter’s Guild to be constructed. This
building represents the pinnacle of the race's military technology, providing troops with training in advanced
fighting techniques and basic battle tactics, enabling the construction of even more sophisticated units. Every
races except Barbarian, Gnoll, Goblin, and Halfling could build this building after casting Tree of Knowledge..
Stables (120 Production, 2 Upkeep) requires Smithy to be constructed. This building serve as breeding grounds
for mounts used by mounted troops, enhancing productivity. They generate +4 Production. Every races except
Dwarf could build this building.
Fantastic Stables (750 Production, 4 Upkeep) requires Stable, and Fighter’s Guild to be constructed. This
building houses and cares for magical beasts, training them to be mounted for warfare. This building is a
requirement for flying mounted units for race that could not naturally fly. This building is only available to cities of
Beastman, Dark Elf, Halfling, High Elf, Nomad, Orc, Xuanyuan, or Rakhshasa race after casting Tree of
Knowledge.
Shipyard (300 Production, 1 Upkeep) requires Dock to be constructed. This building is an upgrade split from old
Dock and Shipyard. This building is a requirement for the city to build more powerful ships. Every race except
Hawkman and Lizardman could build this building.
Maritime Guild (450 Production, 3 Upkeep) requires Shipyard, and Fighter’s Guild to be constructed. This
building facilitates the construction of large ships through training, organization, and support for experienced
shipbuilders. This building is a requirement for the Warship and other ships of similar class. This building is only
available to cities of Barbarian, Draconian, Dwarf, Halfling, High Man, Nomad, Orc, or Xuanyuan race after
casting Tree of Knowledge.
NEW: Hangar (400 Production, 3 Upkeep) requires Sage’s Guild and Mechanician’s Guild to be constructed.
This building is a requirement for mechanical flying units. This building is only available to cities of Draconian,
Goblin, or Hawkman race after casting Tree of Knowledge.
Defensive Structures:
City Walls (90 Production, 1 Upkeep) is a basic city defending structure. This building is surrounding the city
with a tall brick wall that extends the detection range of enemy units to 3 squares. Units positioned behind the
wall gain +3 Armor. If a wall segment is destroyed, this bonus reduces to +1 Armor. The defending side can use
the Disrupt spell to demolish the wall for emergency exits, provided the unit does not already have a spell charge
assigned. Every race except Hawkman could build this building.
NEW: Hillfort (300 Production, 3 Upkeep) requires Miner’s Guild and Stable to be constructed. This building
grants impassable rock cliff face to the city that could not be cross except by Non-Corporeal unit except 4 access
points on each side of the city. The friendly units receive Missile Immunity if the units stay inside city area. This
building is only available to cities of Barbarian, Gnoll, Troll, or Hawkman race.
NEW: Fortification (600 Production, 5 Upkeep) requires City Wall and Mechanician’s Guild to be constructed.
This building grants moat to the city with water terrain that could not cross except with flying or amphibious units
surrounding the city wall except two bridge locations. Friendly units receive bonus equivalent to Large Shield if
they stay inside the city wall area. If the unit already have Large Shield, unit will receive Missile Immunity
instead. This building is only available to cities of Beastman, Dark Elf, Dwarf, Halfling, High Elf, High Man,
Klackon, Orc, or Xuanyuan race after casting Tree of Knowledge.Dock

New Racial Unique Buildings:
Altar of Storm (600 Production, 10 Upkeep) is Barbarian’s unique building that requires Witches’ Convent and
shore nearby the city to be constructed. This building grants the city 8 religious power, and all new units trained
in the city gain the Lightning Blade ability. In combat, the city is protected by a Lightning Storm combat
enchantment.
Idol of Heavenly Bull (1200 Production, 20 Upkeep) is Beastman’s unique building that requires Monastery and
desert nearby the city to be constructed. This building is a significant cult statue revered in beastman culture.
Each worker unit generates 1 food and can receive bonuses from the Animist's Guild. Additionally, all new units
trained in the city gain a 25% increase in Health Points, with a minimum of 1 additional Health Point.
Tree of Magic (1200 Production, 20 Upkeep) is Dark Elf’s unique building that requires Wizard’s Guild and
forest nearby the city to be constructed. This building grants newly trained units with Casting Skill equal to their
base magical Resistance plus base Magic Range Attack at moment they are recruited and all Magic Ranged
units gain +2 Ammo.
Dragon Mound (1200 Production, 10 Upkeep) is Draconian’s unique building that requires Stable and
hill/mountain/volcano nearby the city to be constructed. This building serves as a crucial site for the Draconians
to enhance their dragon powers through communion with the mother drake. Newly trained units from the city
receive significant benefits: they gain +2 Fire Breath and +1 Armor. Additionally, the mother drake's hoard also
serves as an additional Bank, providing provide gold equal to 30% of base Gold generate in the city.
Lava Smelter (1200 Production, 20 Upkeep) is Dwarf’s unique building that requires Alchemist’s Guild and
hill/mountain/volcano nearby the city to be constructed. This building accesses rare minerals by smelting lava
from deep veins beneath hills and mountains. It generates 15 Power and enhances the level of magic weapon
upgrades. At level 1, upgrades Magic weapon into Mithril weapon. At level 2, upgrades Mithril weapon into
Adamantium weapon. At level 3, upgrades Adamantium weapon by give additional Orihalcon upgrade.
Combination of mineral near the city is also grant unit ability. Mithril plus Adamantium grants Weapon Immunity.
Mithril plus Crysx grants Missile Immunity. Mithril plus Orihalcon grants permanent Resist Element. Adamantium
plus Orihalcon grants permanent Elemental Armor. Adamantium plus Crysx grants permanent Flame Blade.
During a siege, the city gains the Wall of Fire enchantment from the outset.
Altar of the Moon (600 Production, 10 Upkeep) is Gnoll’s unique building that requires Witches’ Convent and
swamp nearby the city to be constructed. This building grants the city 8 religious power, all new units gain
Poison Immunity, Rage ability. All ranged units get +2 Ranged Attack. Hunters unit gains Poison 2. And
Witchdoctors unit has Lifesteal -1 replacing its Poison attack. In combat, the city is protected by greater curses.
Academy (1200 Production, 10 Upkeep) is Halfling’s unique building that requires Monastery and
hill/mountain/volcano nearby the city to be constructed. This building is a school dedicated to the study,
discussion, and application of cutting-edge knowledge for public benefit. It provides research based on the
maximum population size, reduces population decrease rate by half, and lowers the cost of ship and siege units
by 25%.
Tree of Life (800 Production, 20 Upkeep) is High Elf’s unique building that requires Animist’s Guild and forest
nearby the city to be constructed. This building accelerates population growth by +100 per month, provides food
equal to the maximum population unit, and grants Regeneration 0 to all defending units in combat that do not
already possess it. It also reduces Unrest by 50% if Wizard's home race is High Elf.
Sancta Basilica (2400 Production, 20 Upkeep) is High Man’s unique building that requires Cathedral and desert
nearby the city to be constructed. This building is housing sacred relics of past Avatars, generates religious
power equal to the city's maximum population unit. All units trained here gain +3 Resistance. Clergy, crusaders,
and paladins receive Sanctify. Crusaders also gain Lucky, paladins gain Magic Immunity, and clergy gain
improved Exorcise but at higher cost. In combat, the city is blessed by True Light.
Undercity Hive Network (1200 Production, 10 Upkeep) is Klackon’s unique building that requires Town Hall
and Mechanician’s Guild to be constructed. This building is an underground settlement and tunnel network
directly beneath the Klackon city. It supports 30% more population capacity but also adds +1 Unrest. Defending
units can move swiftly through the underground tunnels for tactical advantage as if they have Merging ability.
Baray (1000 Production, 10 Upkeep) is Lizardman’s unique building that requires Monastery and river nearby
the city to be constructed. This building is an advanced water system that transforms a dry city into a water
paradise for the Lizardmen. It generates Gold equal to the city's maximum population, reduces Unrest by -2.
Newly trained ground units from this city gain Amphibious and Mariner. In combat, the city area becomes water,
granting all friendly units the ability Amphibious.
Caravanserai (400 Production, 3 Upkeep) is Nomad’s unique building that requires Town Hall and desert
nearby the city to be constructed. This building serves as a crucial station for caravans traversing the desert,
boosting Gold income equivalent to the base trade bonus generated by the city without Nomad bonus. Units
trained in this city, excluding sailing units, gain +2 Overland Movement.
Ludus Agoge (1200 Production, 20 Upkeep) is Orc’s unique building that requires War College and desert
nearby the city to be constructed. This building is an elite school that uses rigorous methods and supplements to
enhance children's performance. The city gains +15 Research points, and new units gain +1 Attack, Resistance,
and Health, except Legionary units, which gain +1 Movement.
Frost Club Hall (600 Production, 10 Upkeep) is Troll’s unique building that requires Brewery and tundra nearby
the city to be constructed. This building aims to restore the prestige and secrets of the Frost Club clan. Newly
trained War Mammoths gain Regeneration 1, and other Troll units gain Cold Immunity and double their
regeneration strength.
Military Workshop (1200 Production, 20 Upkeep) is Xuanyuan’s unique building that requires Mechanician’s
Guild and river nearby to be constructed. This building enables Xuanyuan units to utilize their advanced military
missile technology. All units receive +2 to Physical Ranged, Fire Breath, and Thrown attacks if they possess
those types of attacks, along with a +1 bonus to Poison attacks. Units equipped with Small Physical Ranged
projectiles have them upgraded to gunpowder-infused missiles (Heavy Physical Ranged) instead.
Pool of Repentance (1200 Production, 10 Upkeep) is Rakhshasa’s unique building that requires Monastery and
forest nearby to be constructed. This building is a revered site where rituals of absolution take place. The Pool of
Repentance generates 1 Production for each unit of farmers, reduces Unrest by -3 as a religious building, and
grants new units produced in the city +1 Armor and +1 Resistance.
Altar of the Sun (600 Production, 10 Upkeep) is Hawkman’s unique building that requires Witches’ Convent and
hill/mountain/volcano nearby the city to be constructed. This building grants the city 8 religious power, +100
Population Growth per turn, and all new units except Holy Mother trained in the city gain +1 Figure. In combat,
the city is protected by a High Prayer.
Mother Fungus (1200 Production, 10 Upkeep) is Goblin’s unique building that Witches’ Convent and swamp
nearby the city to be constructed. Goblins all new units gain +2 Attack, +10% to-Defend, Poison 1, and x2
Spellcharge. Additionally, it is detecting all enemies within 10 squares.
Heroes:
To summarize, changes often revolve around making hero stats and abilities fit the theme of races. Discovery is
more exciting than listing all stat changes.
One major overall change is heroes starting with base 40% to hit as a minimum, with some lower stats,
particularly in range, to compensate.
Beastmaster had its fame requirement increased to 10, preventing every single wizard tower to be protected by
a beastmaster hero.
Hero Experience: +5% to hit earned in level 4, level 6, level 8 and level 9 (instead of +10% earned in level 5 and
9)
There's 3 heroes that have unusual item slot configurations: Gunther with 2 swords and no shield, and war monk
and bronze sentinel with no wand/sword (2 accessory slots)
12 heroes have been added: Sagittarius, Crone, Grand Inquisitor, Dwarven Steelbreaker, Elven Dreamwalker,
Halfling Gambler, Gnoll Warmaster, Swarm Queen, King of the Deep, Troll War Chief, Planewalker, Elementalist
Item Costs have been modified to be lower for weakest effects but become more incremental, to balance
against the 'complexity' cost adjustment formula that encourages fewer traits for cost effectiveness. This should
decrease the cost of effects such as +1-2 attack/armor/hp/etc, thus a mixture of weak effects should be similarly
priced than a single stronger effect. Some item ability costs have been adjusted with a few overpriced elements
addressed in this mod. Unfortunately the 'spell charges' continues having a linear cost and being too cheap for
advanced spells.
Attack 50-100-150-250-400-650
- Armor: 75-150-225-375 (Armor caps at +4 for items with just +2 with create item).
- Movement: 250-500-1000
- Resistance: 100-200-300-400-500-600
- Spell Skill: 75-150-225-375
- Spell Save: 200-400-800-1600
- Health: 75-150-300-500-850-1300
- Item flaming ability cost change to 200
- Item destruction ability cost change to 400
- Item wraithform ability cost change to 250 and nolonger and can add with enchant item
- Item bless ability cost change to 150
- Item ability lionheart rename to mystic power, cost increase to 2000 and nolonger need life book
- Item water walking ability cost change to 75
- Item pathfinding ability cost change to 100
- Item resist element ability cost change to 150
- Item regeneration ability cost change to 1000
- Item guardian wind ability cost change to 150
- Item teleporting ability cost change to 900
- Item amplifier ability cost change to 300
- Healing Aura can be added to artifacts at 700 cost
- Binder (spell lock) can be added to artifacts at 700 cost and requires 7 Sorcery books
- Sacred (chosen) can be added to artifacts at 1800 cost and requires 7 Life books
- Colossal Power (iron skin & colossal strength) can be added to artifacts at 1200 cost and requires 5 Nature
books
- Chaos Conduit (blazing march & beat of swiftness) can be added to artifacts at 1200 cost and requires 7
Chaos books
- Plague Lord (causes plague) can be added to artifacts at 1500 cost and requires 7 Death books
- Eye of Storm (lightning storm & hurricane & freezing rain) can be added to artifacts at 1500 cost and requires 7
Nature books
Spell Changes, Comments:
Larger land sizes have a cost modifier to global-type spells (increase)
Larger land sizes have a small cost modifier to localized spells such as unit/city enchantments
(decrease)
There have been changes and additions to give each magic realm more of an identity and playing style.
Note that earliest summons have been all weakened overall and early uncommons now come with higher
research cost. This was done to balance the normal vs fantastic power balance throughout the game,
particularly to address the slower city progression in this mod. Common summons are the least effective tier and
may appear more like being support as opposed to playing entirely with summons (unless conjurer trait),
requiring player to advance to next tier ASAP.
Note that strength of magic attacks are now based on 60% hit chance, rather than 30%.
Common tier spell research costs reduced among spells costing 260 or more, reducing overall research cost of a
realm's 10 commons from 3140 to 2880 (-8%)
Common tier spell research costs shifted around to emphasize strength of certain spells, while staying within the
grand total sum of 2880.
Note that you have 12 uncommon spells and 16 rare spells to choose from, +2 and +4 for each of these tiers,
respectively. In the case of rare-tier spells, arrows are provided to scroll up and down during the 10-book 'early
rare' selection.

Ultimate 330000 Spell of Mastery
Arcane (Generic):
Overall trade value of Arcane spells is decreased due to no wizard that would miss these spells and they would
have those spell sooner or later.
Magic Spirit (cost -/30, 1 upkeep) – the most basic summoning magic, the same as Caster of Magic for
Windows.
Summoning Circle (cost -/0) – Although spell itself is the same as before except for lower trade value (reduced
from 9 to 6), it is no longer guaranteed as early spell for research anymore. This made early gain of this spell by
Conjurer retort more powerful.
Heroic Heart (cost 18/-) – 240 research cost (from 440) – we can't justify such an investment for a healing spell
with ½ the efficiency of life's healing and only limited to heroes. This deserves an average common-tier cost.
Dispel Magic (cost 10+/-) – 320 research cost (from 640) – there needs to be a counter to mega-buffing multi-
figure units early in game, especially in a mod that further encourages buffing normal units. As a result, it was
needed to make dispel magic easily accessible and worth researching early in game.
Enchant Item (cost -/0+) – the spell has lower trade value from Caster of Magic version (from 11 to 9) and
research cost increases to 400 (from 320). The strength of this spell is depending on built the wizards have.
Detect Magic (cost -/200, 3 upkeep) – the spell is lower in trade value (from 11 to 6) but with more expensive
research cost as this spell could be the most important or something you free to ignore depending on what spells
and built the wizards have.
Spell of Return (cost -/1000) – free spell you have from the start in Caster of Magic although it is recognized as
uncommon spell. This spell is a failsafe that as player would not want to be in situation that need this spell but by
having it is still much better than not. So giving it for free is more like helping AI than helping player.
Disenchant Area (cost -/50+, 0 upkeep) – The spell is more or less the same except lower in trade value (from
19 to 17) and some AI behavior about researching it.
Summon Hero (cost -/240) – Trade value of the spell is decreased (from 24 to 20).
Tree of Knowledge (cost -/250) – research cost is increased significantly (from 180 to 2000) due to the city
pacing adjustments (see buildings section) and the more advanced nature of top-tier military units (see military
section, race section), Tree of Knowledge had to be delayed. The higher one-time upfront cost was a preferred
choice over making each of the unlocked buildings take too long to build. Tree of Knowledge unlocks Armorer's
Guild, Fantastic Stables, Maritime's Guild, Wizard's Guild, Hangar, Linking Towers, Amplifying Tower, and racial
unique buildings.
Resurrection (cost -/35, 0 upkeep) – shifted from Life uncommon to arcane rare with 3200 research cost. This
allows all wizards an option to resurrect their fallen hero, but the investment cost is high.
Summon Champion (cost -/600) – trade value of this spell is decreased a bit (from 30 to 28) as there are more
powerful champions to summon but result is also much less reliable as well.
Create Artifact (cost -/0+) – although spell is the same but there are more artifacts ability that could be created
in Warlord mod to design your own custom-made artifacts.
Disjunction (cost -/375+, 0 upkeep) – this spell is more valuable than in Caster of Magic in term of trade value
(from 28 increases to30) as there are more crazy global enchantment that you would want to get rid off here.
Plane Shift (cost -/120, 0 upkeep) – Research cost down to 6000 (from 8000)
Spell of Mastery (cost -/9000+map scaling) – research cost of the spell is lower (from 440000 to 330000) and
arrives a bit earlier to shake things up earlier in game and takes fewer turns to cast, helping put an end to a long
game. Note: Enlightenment spell, which was used to rush-research spell of mastery, was redesigned.
Arcane (Exclusive):
Here are spells which only available to wizard with specific retort. Spells could not be trade or discover in lair,
and have to be research normally to get them. Wizard could get more of them researchable if they earn new
retort during the game.
NEW: Philosopher’s Stone (cost -/210, 7 upkeep) – Split from old sorcery’s Philosopher’s Stone with all
economic part with additional abilities to enchant physical Alchemist’s Guild to generate 12 gold and add mineral
level in place without required mineral. This spell is only available to Alchemist retort holder.
NEW: Education Reform (reform, effect taken upon researched) – All research buildings now generate gold
equal to their upkeep cost. War College also generates additional 2 Research points. This spell is only available
to Sage Master retort holder.
NEW: Arcane Conference (cost -/800, 10 upkeep) – This allow Sage Master to earn additional research from
their own fortress city, +1 for each Library, +2 for each University, +3 for each Sage’s Guild of both planes. This
spell is only available to Sage Master retort holder.
NEW: Wall of Stone (cost -/100, 10 upkeep) – The spell is not only placing physical City Wall, but also
enhanced it to refund their gold upkeep and restore it at the end of opponent turn. But if it destroy in owner turn,
the enchantment will be removed at the end of turn. This spell is only available to Warlord retort holder.
NEW: Mark of Conqueror (cost -/300, 10 upkeep) – The spell is not only placing physical Warlord’s Hold, but
also enhanced it to refund their gold upkeep and restore it at the end of opponent turn. But if it destroy in owner
turn, the enchantment will be removed at the end of turn. This spell is only available to Warlord retort holder.
NEW: Astral Gate (cost -/500, 10 upkeep) – Difference from original version in Master of Magic, this Astral Gate
is one-way portal to other realm. Make sure you could establish outpost on other side for another gate to travel
back. This spell is only available to Myrran retort holder.
NEW: Tactical Drill (cost -/60, 0 upkeep) – Repurpose discipline spell, now it is only castable outside combat.
This spell is only available to Tactician retort holder.
NEW: Tactical Recall (cost 30/-) – Instant spell that allow target unit to escape combat and return with full
health…. if the caster won the combat. If the combat is lost, the recalled unit also destroyed. This spell is only
available to Tactician retort holder.
NEW: Strategic Recall (cost -/100) – Instantly teleport target unit to the Tactician’s fortress. This spell is only
available to Tactician retort holder.
NEW: Marionette (cost -/100) – Summon special hero (the wanderer) at cheap cost and get it early. Hero ability
is customized base on caster’s ability. The hero might not strong but hero could always be resummon after
irrecoverably destroyed and could not permanently die. The spell will temporarily disable if the caster has
Wanderer marionette alive under control. This spell is only available to Channeler retort holder.
NEW: Marionette Ascension (reform, effect taken upon researched) – Upgrade the wanderer hero even further
based on ability of the caster. The wanderer also get stronger as the caster get stronger. This spell is only
available to Channeler retort holder.
NEW: Lord Liberator (reform, effect taken upon researched) – When ever the wizard attack city with race the
same as the wizard own home race, defender suffer -1 Attack/Armor/Resistance. This spell is only available to
Guardian retort holder.
NEW: Lord Protector (reform, effect taken upon researched) – This reform allows guardian retort bonus to
extend to all defending combat. This spell is only available to Guardian retort holder.
Earth Gate Town Portal (cost -/125, 1 upkeep) – Move from Nature realm to Arcane for sake of quality of life in
managing empire in large map. The enchantment is also eliminates gold 'indirect control' penalty of non-capital
cities that get enchanted. This spell is only available to Procurator retort holder.
NEW: Archmage Tutition (reform, effect taken upon researched) – Reform allows all magic user units trained
from fortress city get enhanced in casting skill, spell charge, and ammo if unit have any of these features. This
spell is only available to Archmage retort holder.
NEW: Archmage Guidance (reform, effect taken upon researched) – Reform gives all heroes under the
Archmage wizard to get +40 casting skill. This also applies to heroes who could not casting spell before. This
spell is only available to Archmage retort holder.
NEW: Bountiful Festivity (cost -/75, 2 upkeep) – Alternative spell for population growth and reducing unrest.
This spell is only available to Benefactor retort holder.
NEW: Gospel of Evangelism (cost -/100, 0 upkeep) – Special city curse available to Cult Leader. Garrison units
and city produced less Religious Power depend on Unrest in the city. The more unrest mean the city produce
less power and easy to fall before might of the Cult Leader. This spell is only available to Cult Leader retort
holder.
NEW: Divine Judgement (cost -/1000) – Replacement of Final Wave and Great Unsummoning but instead of
kill indiscriminately, it only damage units under single wizard. This spell is only available to Cult Leader retort
holder.
NEW: Clockwork Tinmen (cost -/120, 5 upkeep) – Summon mechanical engineer unit that could build road very
fast and buff mechanical unit in combat. It ables to destroy any mechanical unit in single hit with its special
ability. This spell is only available to Artificer retort holder.
NEW: Clockwork Factory (cost -/200, 4 upkeep) – Put magical automate factory into the city operate with
magical power and generate 50 production per turn. This spell is only available to Artificer retort holder.
NEW: Rebuild (cost -/150, 0 upkeep) – Permanent unit enchantment that turn unit into mechanical unit with +2
Melee/Armor, Death and Illusion immunity, as well as armor piercing. This spell is only available to Artificer retort
holder.
NEW: Lucky Star (cost 15/-) – Combat unit enchantment that grant Lucky to target unit until the end of combat.
This spell is only available to Astrologer retort holder.
NEW: Dishearten Prophesy (cost -/100, 1 upkeep) – Special city curse available to Astrologer. City suffers +4
unrest and garrisons suffer -2 Resistance in combat. This spell is only available to Astrologer retort holder.
NEW: Conjuring Pact (cost 40/-) – Attempts to tame fantastic creature. If non-fantastic creature get hit by this
would suffer nausea (-10 To-Hit/To-Defend). If tamed fantastic creature survive the combat, Conjurer could
research how to summon them if their realm proficieny is high enough (at least twice of normal rarity level). This
spell is only available to Conjurer retort holder.
NEW: Spirit Link (cost -/150, 0 upkeep) – Turn unit into non-fantastic creature while still able to receive bonus
as if they are fantastic creatures and get additional +2 Resistance. Unit that originally don’t have experience
level now also able to gain experience level and could be enchanted with normal unit enchantment while unable
to be targeted by spell that only affects fantastic creature. This spell is only available to Conjurer retort holder.
NEW: Rally (cost 15/-) – All friendly unit get +2 Resistance until the end of combat. This spell is only available to
Charismatic retort holder.
NEW: Denoucement (cost -/200) – Deal damage to reputation of the wizard who own target city and reduces
their standing among the wizard. This spell is only available to Charismatic retort holder.
NEW: Whispering Echo (cost 150/-) – Attempts to convince all opponents units in combat to switch side or at
least sows discord and confusion among them. Strength of the spell depend on caster has Charismtic or
Charming or not. This spell is only available to Charismatic retort holder.
NEW: Tattoo Magic (reform, effect taken upon researched) – Reform allows all newly trained unit with non-
permanent enchantment to become permanent enchantment and could not be dispelled. This spell is only
available to Enchanter retort holder.
NEW: Domain of Enchanter (cost -/800, 10 upkeep) – This global enchantment enhances dispel resistance of
all enchantment of the caster twice its strength. All unit curses cast by the Enchanter will become permanent and
would not dispelled at the end of combat. This spell is only available to Enchanter retort holder.
NEW: Tabula Rasa (cost 100/-) – This combat enchantment will removed enemy’s combat enchantments again
and again at chance of 33% at the beginning of the Caster’s turn. This spell is only available to Runemaster
retort holder.
NEW: Rune Formation Array (cost -/1200, 100 upkeep) – This spell is repurposed of Caster of Magic’s original
Power Link. The size of battery is now reduced to 5000. This spell is only available to Runemaster retort holder.
Nature:
Nature realm is about adaptability and making the best of the world terrain and minerals. If playing a mono-realm
wizard, Nature is the least specialized realm. However, the player is more likely to have the necessary tools to
do an adequate job on most circumstances.
There have been some additions to unit, city and global enchantments with direct or indirect boosts to unit
recruitment strategies, thus conjurer is no longer a near-mandatory retort for nature players.
New spells further establish these realm characteristics.
Removed Nature Spells
Fairy Dust – To emphasize realm uniqueness of chaos, removed this spell as researchable but still using by
Sacred Ancient (see uncommon spell below). This spell was potentially more damaging than fireball! Nature
creature casters can still cast fairy dust.
Earth Gate Town Portal (cost -/125, 1 upkeep) – Move to Procurator’s signature. The spell is replacing by new
global enchantment “Ice Age”
Nature Common Spells
Earth Lore (cost -/10) – Same as in vanilla Caster of Magic for Windows
Nature's Eye Nature's Witness (cost -/35, 0 upkeep) – In addition to current effects, grants 4 power and -1
unrest If nightshade present.
Water Walking (cost -/20, 0 upkeep) – Research cost decreases from 260 to 240.
Earth to Mud (cost 20/-) – Research cost increases from 280 to 380.
Wild Boars (cost 15/-, 1 upkeep) – Research cost increases from 280 to 320.
War Bears (cost -/65, 2 upkeep) – Now with 2 figures and higher cost, but with increased melee and hp per
figure.
NEW: Sprites Killer Wasps (cost -/55, 1 upkeep) – replaces sprites and maintain a role of being a particularly
good unit against lairs/nodes/neutrals but unreliable against wizards. Wasps have useful early perks like 9-
figures, missile immunity, and high armor (with 1hp) allowing it to reroll armor every time it loses 1 hp. It benefits
greatly from melee and hp buffs. With base stats, it is mainly a low-damaging annoyance that also serves as a
counter against bowmen. The unit has been revisited due to claims that it is overpowered. War Bears are more
reliable, but wasps have more potential under the right circumstances.
Resist Elements (cost 5/25, 0 upkeep) – Research cost decreases from 440 to 320.
Web (cost 10/-) – Research cost decreases from 480 to 400.
NEW: Survival of The Fittest Natural Selection (cost -/150, 3 upkeep) – Global Common - Units trained gain
bonus based on resources in the recruiting town's surroundings including coal (+1 melee), iron (+1 armor), wild
games (+1 ranged attack and gain forester), nightshade (+1 resistance). And power minerals (+1 resist per 10
base power income from minerals). This replaces 'fairy dust' and is more consistent with Nature's theme of
benefiting from terrain.
NEW: Wargs (cost -/64, 1 upkeep) – This spell could only be learned with Conjuring Pact and 2 Nature spell
books.
NEW: Sprites (cost -/70, 2 upkeep) – This spell could only be learned with Conjuring Pact and 2 Nature spell
books.
Nature Uncommon Spells
Land Linking → Nature Link (cost 13/65, 1 upkeep) – Renamed from Land Linking. Spell is castable in combat
and also grants an additional +1 resistance to the enchanted unit (whether normal or fantastic). Rush-research
can be a beneficial tactic.
NEW: Venom (cost 12/60 1 upkeep) – Uncommon – target unit gains poison immunity and +1 poison. Please
note that poison can trigger during ranged and thrown attacks, thus you have a chance of inflicting poison twice
when attacking or once from a distance. The poison immunity benefit may be what draws you to this spell,
especially early in game as your low-resistance units get damaged too easily by too-common sources of poison.
Giant Spiders (cost -/110, 2 upkeep) – The unit, while costlier, comes with an extra charge of 'web', greatly
expanding its use as a support unit throughout the game. Early uncommon summon strategies weakened to
make normal units more relevant, thus spider's research cost has been more than doubled.
Change Terrain (cost -/28) – Research cost increases from 960 to 1000.
Nature’s Cure (cost -/50) – Research cost decreases from 1280 to 1100.
Ice Bolt (cost 24/-) – Now spell’s cost reduces from 25 to 24 so the spell can be accessed by ultra elite caster 20
units. Strength of attack reduces by half (from 34 to 17) but double hit chance (30% to 60%). Trade value is also
increased.
Cockatrices (cost -/150, 4 upkeep) – Although spell cost is still the same, cockatrices’s stone touch is no longer
able to be triggered by magic ranged attack, so it loses combo with Focus Magic spell.
Iron Skin (cost 21/105, 3 upkeep) – Change from rare to uncommon spell, research cost decreases from 4000
to 1400, and casting cost reduces from 24/120 to 21/105.
Water Elemental (cost 40/-, 3 upkeep) – moved from sorcery as an uncommon nature combat summon,
replacing the poor 'construct catapult'. The unit was appropriately adjusted with deal less damage, particularly its
ranged attacks. While stats may appear underwhelming, this unit should not be underestimated in the hands of a
smart player with the right set of support spells and under the right circumstances (and can also be a good
desperate combat spell for a poorly defended city under siege).
Crack's Call (cost 30/-) – Spell now calculates damage and burying chance differently and gives additional
penalties to buried units. It now calculates chance to bury unit at 4% * unit armor chance, capped at 75%. A unit
that is buried suffers -20% to defend in this mod. Burying a high-armor unit, rather than chance at damage, is
more reliable and helps with defensive stalling. Damage is less dangerous in this mod, dealing 4 rolls of 25%
chance at dealing 4 points of damage each (if unit is buried, two additional rolls take place)
Transmute (cost -/60) – Research cost increases from 1920 to 2000.
Great Lizard (cost -/200, 5 upkeep) – Given water walking (why wouldn't a great lizard swim?) and ability to
blend in nature (stealth) as well as a few damage from poison attack.
Nature Rare Spells
Gaia’s Blessing (cost -/100, 3 upkeep) – Trade value increases.
NEW: Transmute Equipment (cost -/90, 0 upkeep) – Rare. Pseudo unit enchantment that gives adamantium
and orihalcon to a normal unit or grant permanent buff to a hero. There's a chance you may have many
experienced units recruited before you transmuted minerals to adamantium – this is your chance to provide that
to them. With this spell, you can permanently buff your heroes with similar value as what normal unit gains as
well.
Earthquake (cost -/150) – Still the same as in Caster of Magic for WIndows.
Elemental Armor (cost 18/90, 1 upkeep) – Research cost reduces from 3200 to 3000, trade value is also
reduced.
NEW: Colossal Strength (cost 24/120, 3 upkeep) – Rare unit enchantment that increases melee and physical
ranged strength by 40%. A new opportunity to buff heroes in nature and help make your single figure summons
capable of damaging more units.
Blizzard (cost -/120) – Trade value increases but attack strength reduces from 14 to 12 and research cost
reduces from 4000 to 3500.
NEW: Sacred Ancient (cost 32/-, 0 upkeep) – Uncommon combat summon. Immobile support units that grant
+1 resist to all, have 'fairy dust' charges, and very high durability stats. This spell helps with defensive stalling,
grants much-needed resistance, and grants nature a chance to use the otherwise-disabled 'fairy dust' when
suitable multi-figure targets are your threat and randomly freeze them to skip a turn. This unit is disabled as
rampaging monster. This immobile unit may be obtainable from the very rare global enchantment 'Fairy Ring'. If
so, Sacred Ancient generates power income outside combat.
Stone Giant (cost -/250, 5 upkeep) – lowered cost to 250 to ensure nature's summon superiority doesn't solely
depend on its only rare-tier 'Survival Instinct'. Its impressive stats for the low cost make this a good spell
adaptable to most situations.
Abundance (cost -/150, 2 upkeep) – This enchantment is also additionally eliminated overfarming penalty from
the city. Research cost increases from 3600 to 4000.
Petrify (cost 20/-) – Research cost reduces from 4400 to 4000.
NEW: Freezing Rain (cost 45/-) – At the end of each turn, each opponent's unit get hit by fairy dust-like attack.
Units that do not have Cold Immunity, Non-Corporeal, or Immolation have a 50% chance to be frozen and fixed
to the ground until the end of the next turn.
NEW: Thunderbird (cost 350/7) - Rare. Giant eagle with strong lightning breath (activates only when attacking).
The thunderbird is also immune to Hurricane (see below). This is the only relatively advanced flying unit offered
by Nature.
Earth Elemental (cost 50/-, 4 upkeep) – Spell is cheaper to research (5600 to 4600) but also reduces in trade
value. Earth Elemental is now also get bonus based on resource of the combat tile on overland and what kind of
terrain that Earth elemental summon upon in combat.
Gorgons (cost -/320, 8 upkeep) – Slightly lower stats across the board, loses supernatural, and cheaper. Now
this is the nature unit with 40 caster, shifted from behemoth. Gorgon is generally more usable after this change
and can be optimized by having it cast petrify spell twice. This is also to ensure summon superiority of nature not
being as dependent on rare-tier 'Survival Instinct'
Survival Instinct (cost -/600, 15 upkeep) – For flavor, newly created normal units also gain small stat boosts
based on city's surroundings: 'to defend' (+3% to +7%) based on gold-producing resources (which may be
transmuted to mithril/adamantium otherwise).
NEW: Hurricane (cost 30/-) – Rare, Reduces Ranged to Hit by 20% and breath to hit by 30% to all units
including casting wizard. Eliminates flying to all units (except thunderbird and air elemental) including casting
wizard's. Nature wizards are least vulnerable to these effects, especially wizards dominating with ground melee
units, thus serving as a useful counter at a low cost against specific threats such as dragon units. Enemy AI is
fairly smart when cast this spell to its advantage.
Call The Wild – Nature Embrace (cost -/900, 30 upkeep) – In addition to the existing rampaging monster and
lair guardian effects, all newly recruited units start with 'resist elements' if the recruiting town has an animist guild
built.
NEW: Ice Comet (cost 50/-) – Drop a gigantic ice comet at a target unit, This spell is acting as single target non-
magical multifigure attack and also act as multi-target single turn freeze debuff too.
Nature Very Rare or Higher Spells
Clairvoyance (cost -/800, 20 upkeep) – Costlier but now also comes with an unrest quelling effect (2 rebels) to
accommodate the higher population of 'abundance' cities and be able to more effectively protect against unrest-
causing spells.
Regeneration (cost 32/160, 5 upkeep) – Research cost reduces from 12000 to 8000.
Fairy Ring (cost -/1200, 40 upkeep) – Now also grants 10 flat overland skill bonus plus 1 for every animist guild
in towns controlled by casting wizard.
Great Wyrm (cost -/450, 15 upkeep) – Reduced cost and given higher movement and water walking.
NEW: Ice Age (cost -/1500, 100 upkeep) – This new global enchantment, replacing Earth Gate that move to
Arcane, is Nature’s equivalent of Doomsday by causing climate change that causing changing in combat
landscape, both land and sea, and reduce food production worldwide. As productive land gradually turns into
tundra while once useless land of your empire turn into productive land. Additionally caster is coming into
combat with free Freezing Rain and their nature creature gain cold immunity while all opponent sailing units
losing 50% of movement points due to erratic wind pattern tha they could not handle.
Herb Mastery (cost -/1000, 12 upkeep) - Herb Mastery has two added effects: it increases overall population
growth of cities by +33% while halving pop reducing effects, a soft counter to Death realm. Nature has many
tools to increase your maximum population capacity, but we need this to make it easier to reach those
maximums.
Call Lightning – Lightning Storm (cost 65/-) –lightning bolts are now strength 7 (60% hit chance)
Behemoth (cost -/550, 14 upkeep) – Costlier and without caster 40, but given even higher offense and defense
stats and abilities (e.g. armor piercing, cause fear) as well as a stoning gaze of -4 which helps unit hit flyers. It
can also walk on water.
Planetary Mastery (cost -/1000, 30 upkeep) – higher research cost and upkeep but now also doubles mineral
bonuses to all cities (similar to Dwarf racial bonus), further establishing Nature realm as one dependent on the
quality of your territory.
Colossus (cost -/500, 15 upkeep) – Now has higher movement and +10% to defend, but lower ammo and
higher cost.
Entangle (cost 50/-) – still the same as in Caster of Magic for WIndows.
Roots of Genesis (cost -/1200, 30 upkeep) – also has additional effect of spawning wild games in forest tiles
and tundra tiles and nightshades in river tiles within city area of the caster at rate of 0.5% per tile.
NEW: Gaia Mastery (reform, effect taken upon researched) – Increases enchantment dispel resistance, reduces
casting cost of the spells, and buff creature of the Nature realm under wizard control. This reform is only
available to Specialist retort holder with Nature as primary realm. Once this spell appears on research page, it
will exclude chance to get mastery of other realm.
NEW: Lesser Gaia Lord (cost -/777, 20 upkeep) – This spell could only be learned with Conjuring Pact and 10
Nature spell books.
NEW: Great Gaia Lord (cost -/999, 30 upkeep) – This spell could only be learned with Conjuring Pact and 12
Nature spell books.
NEW: Power of Nature (cost 105/-) – This spell could only be learned by Enchanter wizard who already have
access to Resist Elements, Water Walking, Nature Link, Venom, Colossal Strength, Elemental Armor, Iron Skin,
and Regeneration. This spell would allow the Enchanter to cast all above unit enchantment all at once on single
target!
NEW: Force of Nature (cost 150/-) – This spell could only be learned by Runemaster wizard who already have
access to Lightning Storm, Entangle, Freezing Rain, and Hurricane. This spell would allow the Runemaster to
cast all above combat enchantment all at once!
Sorcery:
Sorcery realm specializes in utility spells, negating enemy magic, and illusionist trickery. It rewards opportunistic
players.
The realm has several means of expanding your abilities as a wizard, whether it is power income, casting skill,
gold.
Many spells act as a reaction of a situation, often to shut down threats or bring gameplay mechanics in your
favor: ground troops threatening your city? Hold them in place or make your city fly! A spell threatens your
game? Counter or dispel it! Don't want to lose a unit or a city to spells in a game revolving around magic? Make
them universally immune! At its most powerful, Sorcery can stop time itself. These are generally defensive tools
for cautious wizards. The Sorcery school of magic also carries naval advantages with this mod's new spells.
The dispelling nature of Sorcery also applies to banishing creatures altogether. Meanwhile, sorcery summoners
have a wide variety of highly strategic combat and overland summons and thus are good candidates for
Conjurer retort.
New spells further establish these realm characteristics.
Removed Sorcery Spells
Old Seravy Version of Power Link is removed due to its capabilities to break entire game is it is coming early
with several wizards still active.
Great Unsummoning is removed due to it cause end turn exceptionally long during its processing of result.
Sorcery Common Spells
Floating Island (cost -/45, 1 upkeep) – the spell is the same as in Caster of Magic but the unit able to be
upgraded upon summon by later Mariner Mastery.
Guardian Wind (cost 6/30, 1 upkeep) – trading value is increased from 6 to 7.
AEther Spark (cost 12/-) – attack strength change from 20 at 30% hit chance to 10 at 60% hit chance and
research cost decreases from 260 to 240.
Nagas (cost -/65, 1 upkeep) – reduced in cost and upkeep to slightly improve early sorcery game on this front
relative to other realms, but overall stats decreased (-1 melee, -1hp). Nagas (amphibious) gain faster movement
and fire immunity while fighting in an ocean tile.
Phantom Warriors (cost -/65, 1 upkeep) – research cost decreases from 320 to 280.
Vertigo (cost 10/-) – the spell change to common level and reduction in trade value (from 15 to 11) as well as
research cost (from 640 to 280) to common level.
Resist Magic (cost 8/40, 0 upkeep) – research cost decreases from 320 to 280.
Psionic Blast (cost 20/-) – attack strength change from 18 at 30% hit chance to 11 at 60% hit chance and
research cost decreases from 380 to 360.
Blur (costs 24/-) – trade value decreases from 19 to 16 but now cost of the spell is decreased from 25 to 24 and
has stronger synergy with invisibility (top up damage reduction change from 10% to 20%)
Aura of Majesty (cost -/200, 12 upkeep) – now common-tier but player should double-check before investing on
a 12 upkeep spell early on. This was the most appropriate spell to move to common based on the focus magic
change.
Sorcery Uncommon Spells
Focus Magic (cost 16/80, 2 upkeep) – now uncommon-tier due to later access to mage-type units and to
increase difficulty in successfully applying overpowered combos with other realms. The unit enchantment also
felt too advanced and complex to be a common spell, but relative to other changes in this mod, this spell was too
limited in use early in the game (casting it on nagas is not as good as it appears). Stoning (and death) touch also
no longer can apply in ranged attacks. This eliminates 'focus magic cockatrices' combo. You cannot 'touch' with
ranged attacks, makes 0 logical sense. The spell get compensated by new ability to cast in combat, +1
maximum spell charge, and increase of trade value from 12 to 20.
Confusion (cost 16/-) – the spell is moving up from common to uncommon with lower casting cost (from 18 to
16) and higher save penalty (from -2 to -3) with research cost increases from 320 to 700.
Aether Binding (cost -/300, 15 upkeep) – Cost decreased but the dispelling strength effect is halved. It is now a
mostly economical spell. The doubled dispel power was moved to the new Power Link.
Flight (cost 22/110, 2 upkeep) – the spell is the same except for research cost is lower from 1280 to 1000.
NEW: Mariner Mastery (cost -/250, 8 upkeep) – Uncommon Global that permanently grants +2 move to all
sailing units and mechanical flying ships (when recruited) and floating island and +1 to water walking units during
combat as long as spell is active, granting sorcery a naval advantage over other realms
Water Elemental Coatl (cost -/150, 3 upkeep) – replaces water elemental (Which was moved to nature as
combat summon replacing Construct Catapult). This mobile, flying unit with low caster points is meant to be
tactical flying cavalry but not very good in stats alone thus not intended to be used as a brute force unit. Caster
ability helps it self-cast Guardian Wind or Resist Magic or AEether sparks depending on circumstance.
Spell Lock (cost -/100, 1 upkeep) – the spell is the same as in Caster of Magic for Windows
Philosopher’s Stone Magic Perimeter (cost -/75, 1 upkeep) – Although it still give magic weapon to newly
trained unit, it does not give access to ore utilization. Note: counter magic has also been weakened to strength
60 (from 70).
Counter Magic (cost 40/-) – Cheaper casting cost of 40 (instead of 50) and lower research cost to 1600 (from
2140) but weaker with starting counter strength of 60 (instead of 70).
Phantom Beast (cost 35/-, 2 upkeep) – research cost increases to 1800 (from 1600).
Dispelling Wave (cost 25+/-) – research cost increases to 2000 (from 1920).
NEW: Magocracy (cost -/400, 20 upkeep) – Uncommon Global. All caster cities gain gold from magic markets
and wizard guilds equivalent to their power income (base 4 and 12, respectively). Sorcery has many tools to help
you progress as a wizard and this has the capacity of increasing your gold income by triple digits.
Sorcery Rare Spells
Disillusionise (cost -/50+) – trade value reduced to 24 (from 28) and research cost decreases to 2400 (from
4000)
NEW: Aether Sink (cost -/100, 2 upkeep) – Rare city curse, Cuts non-religious power (minimum=5) and skill
income from city in half, making you even stronger as a wizard relative to opponents.
Flying Fortress (cost -/200, 3 upkeep) – research cost increases to 2800 (from 2400)
Spell Blast (cost -/50) – research cost decreases to 3000 (from 5600)
Stasis (cost 35/175) – the spell get significantly more expensive but coming with a impressively stronger -7
resistance modifier.
Invisibility (cost 30/150, 6 upkeep) – research cost is decreased to 3500 (from 3600) and has stronger internal
synergy with Blur (damage reduction top up increases from 10% to 20%).
NEW: Kraken (cost -/310, 8 upkeep) – Rare summon. A swimming creature with high melee and defense stats.
Kraken specializes at hunting down transport ships: while at sea it gains stealth and in battles situated at sea (+3
move, fire immunity, invisible, +10% to defend), giving Sorcery realm further naval advantages.
Reinforce Magic (cost -/500, 25 upkeep) – trade value increases to 34 (from 33)
Banish (cost 40/-) – get more powerful with -5 resistance modifier and higher trade value (from 25 to 26).
Mind Storm (cost 35/-) – research cost reduces to 4000 (from 4800)
NEW: Sea Serpent (cost 75/-, 15 upkeep) – rare combat summons. Sea Serpent is a rare level creature with
strengtth as strong as very rare level fantastic creature but could only be summoned on water tile. Apart from
usage for naval combat, it might be useful in defending some city with Fortification or Baray.
Air Elemental (cost 50/-, 5 upkeep) – research cost reduces to 4300 (from 4400)
NEW: Cloud Giant (cost -/330, 9 upkeep) – replaces storm giant. This is a different version that attacks with
illusion, flies, and has 'lucky' trait. Its stats were significantly lower to balance out these enhancements, resulting
in a summon of comparable usefulness to storm giant, just modified to fit the nature of 'sorcery'.
Wind Walking (cost -/200, 7 upkeep) – ability of Wind Walking enchanment is now called “High Wind Walking”
to separate from version without overland movement bonus. Research cost decreases to 4900 (from 5200)
NEW: Temporal Twist (cost 40/-) – Rare combat global enchantment – all enemy units lose 1 movement,
teleport, first strike, and negate first strike. If the unit is fantastic, it loses an additional movement point. Speed
reduces by Temporal Twist would not cause unit speed to go below 0.5. There isn't a counter to first
strike/negate first strike in this game and this spell is ideal against summons, something Sorcery is good against.
NEW: Aether Surge (cost 60/-) – Rare combat global enchantment. All caster's units in combat gain +10 casting
skill, this includes units which originally does not have casting MP. Each turn, current MP would have MP
replenish at rate 5 MP per turn and spell charge would be recharged every 4 turns until the end of combat.
Uranus Blessing (cost -/225, 7 upkeep) – redesigned to grant power equal to city's research income, which can
include buildings, town population, enchantments, sorcery procurator. Cost increased to compensate. The
overland skill bonus is now granted by various research buildings instead of just amplifier tower. This spell
caught a lot of attention for combo potential, but players attempting to maximize combos unintentionally
introduce vulnerabilities. If you manage to pull this off with good synergies, this can win you the game.
NEW: Planewalking (cost 30/150, 8 upkeep) – rare unit enchantment, allow unit to plane shift freely on overland
map and teleport movement in combat.
NEW: Storm Giant (cost -/330, 5 upkeep) – This spell could only be learned with Conjuring Pact and 6 Sorcery
spell books.
Sorcery Very Rare or Higher Spells
Creature Binding (cost 55/-) – buffed with -5 resistance modifier. It was underwhelming that sorcery could kill
fantastic creatures at -3 in entire world, death could possess a unit at -3 with an uncommon-tier spell, but sorcery
with a single target spell has merely 1 more resistance modifier. This comes with higher research cost of 8000
(from 6000) and higher trade value (from 28 to 38)
Spell Ward (cost -/150, 1 upkeep) – nothing has changed for this spell but more synergy to feed new Power
Link.
NEW: Great Unbinding (cost -/1000, 50 upkeep) – powerful very rare global enchantment to replace time
ravaging Great Unsummoning. At the beginning of combat all opponent fantastic creatures that participate in
combat against the caster have to face Confusion curse with -4 resistance penalty, and even if survive that they
still have to deal with significant debuff of -20% To-Hit, -20% To-Defend, and -2 Resistance for the rest of
combat.
Haste (cost 50/200, 8 upkeep) – now castable overland with 200 cost and 8 upkeep. Overland movement not
impacted, only combat movement. This spell effectively doubles your attack strength while granting a unit so
much mobility that almost matches teleport. If you can afford the cost, you can save combat turns by casting and
maintaining this spell outside of battle.
Djinn (cost -/395, 10 upkeep) – Now comes with caster 40, helping it cast the stronger banish spell, temporal
twist and not be behind efreet's caster capabilities.
Magic Immunity (cost 45/180, 10 upkeep) – higher casting cost prevents Djinn from self-casting (unless buffed
with focus magic)
Wind Mastery (cost -/900, 30 upkeep) – the same as before with minor tweak in AI behavior.
Sky Drake (cost -/500, 15 upkeep) – gains mountaineer for sake of synergy with tactician retort, research cost
increased to 16000 (from 15000).
Spell Binding (cost -/1200) – research cost decreases to 18000 (from 22000)
Mass Invisibility (cost 80/-) – the same as in Caster of Magic for Windows except for now synergy with Blur is
stronger (damage reduction top up increases to 20% from formerly 10%)
NEW: Power Link (cost -/1200, 50 upkeep) – Power Link has been completely changed, including spell image.
It now
• grants 5 power per city enchantment (15 if city curse) in all your cities
• grants 2 overland skill per enemy Amplifying Tower in play
• grants full effect of all enemy monuments and linking towers to your combat skill
• makes dispel-type spells +100% effective. If combined with Aether Binding, it simulates old game's
'True' dispel spells.
• Eliminates non-capital power income penalty
Reason: The original spell was too 'mathematical', caused variable power spikes that could heavily impact
domination score and the 'win' button, was too overpowered if obtained early or there are too many players, and
didn't seem to affect enemy spell decision logic. The new Power Link has more strategic components while still
scaling reasonably well with more players.
Time Stop (cost -/1500, +50 upkeep per turn, +250 upkeep per city taken during Time Stop,) – apart from lower
casting cost but higher upkeep, research cost decreases to 22000 (from 24000), combat during Time Stop
changes with all opponent units in combat have to resist at -7 or suffered Stasis, no normal overland damage
recovery, and casting skill decay by 3% each turn (capped at not lower than 10%, will recovered once Time Stop
is no longer maintained) while cast cost of spell increases by 1% for each spell cast during Time Stop. So now
Time Stop becomes more combat-oriented and reduced number of things that could be done if maintaining the
spell for too long and finishing Spell of Mastery during Time Stop is nigh impossible.
NEW: Cloud Elephant (cost -/550, 15 upkeep) – This spell could only be learned with Conjuring Pact and 8
Sorcery spell books.
