NEW: AEther Mastery (reform, effect taken upon researched) – Increases enchantment dispel resistance,
reduces casting cost of the spells, and buff creature of the Sorcery realm under wizard control. This reform is
only available to Specialist retort holder with Sorcery as primary realm. Once this spell appears on research
page, it will exclude chance to get mastery of other realm.
NEW: Lesser AEther Lord (cost -/777, 20 upkeep) – This spell could only be learned with Conjuring Pact and
10 Sorcery spell books.
NEW: Great AEther Lord (cost -/999, 30 upkeep) – This spell could only be learned with Conjuring Pact and 12
Sorcery spell books.
NEW: Power of Sorcery (cost 160/-) – This spell could only be learned by Enchanter wizard who already have
access to Resist Magic, Guardian Wind, Flight, Focus Magic, Planewalking, Invisibility, Haste, and Magic
Immunity. This spell would allow the Enchanter to cast all above unit enchantment all at once on single target!
NEW: Mystery of Sorcery (cost 150/-) – This spell could only be learned by Runemaster wizard who already
have access to Blur, Counter Magic, Aether Surge, Temporal Twist, and Mass Invisibility. This spell would allow
the Runemaster to cast all above combat enchantment all at once!
Chaos:
Chaos realm specializes in blitzkrieg tactics with mobile units that excel in offense and combat spells that
quicken the pace of combat for earlier resolution. Combat spells are prominent and often focus on damaging
individual units and armies.
Later in game, chaos is also aggressive against cities as well as terrain, sabotaging enemy economically on a
global scale with caster wizard gaining benefits from such effects at the same time.
New spells further establish these realm characteristics.
Removed Chaos Spells
Flame Blade (becomes unit ability) – grants +3 melee, +2 physical range/thrown, and +1 fire breath (granting
ability to hit flyers). This ability could nolonger able to be countered by anything but Chaos Ward. This ability can
only be cast by dwarf combat engineers.
Berserk (becomes unit ability) – completely new spell and not relate to original’s Berserk. Target unit gains
+15% To-Hit and +1 combat Movement but suffers -10% To-Defend. Could only be casted by Troll
Medicinemans.
Fate Mastery → Dance of Death. The spell felt misplaced in chaos realm and not worth keeping just to
introduce a chaos+death combo. The spell is move to Death realm at rare tier.
Warp Lightning → Lightning Rage (cost 30/-) – Warp Lightning is renamed to Lightning Rage and only
available to the Warlock hero.
Chaos Common Spells
Hell Hounds (cost -/54, 1 upkeep) – Boosted to have 5 movement and slightly higher cost (from 40 to 48), it acts
relatively similar to a barbarian cavalry unit – great for exploration and to reach the other side of the battlefield in
2 moves. This fits the theme of chaos being an aggressive magic realm and speed is an element that adds to its
aggressive nature. The cost effectiveness brings back the original MoM starting game chaos hell hound spam
strategies.
Animate Ammo (cost 5/-) – Research cost decreases to 280 (from 320).
Corruption (cost -/30) – Reduced cost by 10 given more options for units with purify ability and faster roads to
move them where needed. Research cost also decreases to 240 (from 260).
Fire Bolt (cost 9/-) – Attack strength of Fire Bolt reduces from 24 to 12 but hit chance is doubled (from 30% to
60%). Spell’s research cost is reduced to 280 (from 320). The spell’s cost get lowered (from 10 to 9) to ensure
chaos is best realm at direct damage.
Wall of Fire (cost 30/60, 1 upkeep) – Instead of 10-strength to all figures, it is 12-strength (60% hit chance) but
not on all figure. It also grants +1 attack to all defending normal unit non-magic attacks, similar to original game's
Metal Fires. Wall of fire now costs 30 to cast while in combat (from 20), has 1 upkeep (from previously 0),
reduced in trade value, and its research cost is reduced to 280 (from 320).
Warp Creature (cost 10/-) – spell research cost is reduced to 320 (from 380) but trade value is increased as the
spell get upgrade to be cursed by 3 types of warp creature effects at once once caster casted Doom Mastery.
Shatter – Spell move to rare tier to allow room for the similar but more interesting 'Rust'
NEW Rust (cost 7/-) – common-tier combat unit curse. Resistance roll of -5 penalty. If successful:
• Unit with magic weapons or orihalcon lose those bonuses permanently, have regular weapons
• Unit loses 3 of its physical attack
• All thrown attack is eliminated until end of combat
• Large shield, if present, is eliminated until end of combat.
Rust is the only spell in the game that invalidates magic weapons altogether – the strategies around weapon
immunity bring significant synergy with death.
Flame Blade Fiery Fury (cost 10/50, 1 upkeep) – Now also grants +2 to all non-magic, non-elemental ranged
attack types, and thrown, not just some ranged attack types. Also, if cast on a fantastic creature, it turns that
creature into chaos (thus benefiting from chaos global effects) and gives first strike. Research cost of the spell is
cheaper than Flame Blade (360 compared to Flame Blade’s 480) and has a bit more trade value.
NEW Blaze of Glory (cost 20/-) – Combat only unit enchantment – shifts armor points to melee, ranged points
also to melee, grants armor piercing, but enchanted unit loses first strike (if present). This is similar in spirit to the
original game's berserk, but chaos tends to be the most 'reckless' realm, thus fitting here. It is one of the
common-tier combat spells that is powerful throughout game (just like web)
Breakthrough (cost 9/-) – This new combat enchantment is made by Seravy as replacement of the most
useless spell to be casted by wizard in game, Disrupt. The spell has multiple effect which is basically enchant
melee attack, especially to combat summon and Non-Corporeal units, and grant all units Wall Crashing ability.
Chaos Uncommon Spells
Gargoyles (cost -/100, 1 upkeep) – The creature is more or less the same with research cost increases to 500
(from previously 420) and a little bit lower trade value.
Chaos Channels (cost -/50, 0 upkeep) – The spell is increased in trade value and research cost also increased
to 700 (from 640). Fire breath version is now also stack with unit original fire breath. If caster has Doom Mastery,
this spell will grants all three effects instead of just one.
Fire Elemental (cost 24/-, 2 upkeep) – Moved to uncommon, given immolation, higher hp, and changed its
attack pattern to be entirely 'fire breath' oriented. The 'weapon immunity' early game design is now exclusive to
death realm, while chaos is allowed to excel at the start with combat spells.
Immolation (cost 13/65, 2 upkeep) – Now costs 13/65 (from 12/60) due to considered as superior than Fireball,
but trade value is decreased to 9 (from 10) and research cost is reduced to 1000 (from 1280) as opportunity to
use the spell is lower.
Fire Giant (cost -/110, 3 upkeep) – Fireball spell removed, added +1 range and +1 ammo, +1 armor, +2hp, and
large shield. Research cost is reduced to 1100 (from 1280) but trade value of the spell is increased to 20 (from
17).
Raise Volcano (cost -/50) – The spell is more or less the same but volcano is now more useful terrain with
recent combo with Chaos’ Blessing (+3 power) and Ice Age (+1 Max Population) as well as there are more use
of mineral that caster could get from spawning volcano.
Fireball (cost 19/-) – Now strength is increased to 14 (from 12) but with cost increase. Needed more strength to
justify its research cost that is also increased to 1280 (from 960).
Lightning Bolt (cost 24/-) – Now costs is decreased to 24 (from previously 25) so it could be accessed by ultra
elite caster 20 units. Attack strength is changed to strength 18 at 60% To-Hit (from previously strength 36 at 30%
To-Hit) to make damage more consistent and reliable. Research cost is also decreased to 1400 (from 1600).
NEW: Insulation (cost 16/80, 2 upkeep) – New uncommon unit enchantment that provides fire immunity, cold
immunity, and lightning resistance. Situationally useful with an obvious combo with Inner Power, but fairly
expensive and situational otherwise.
NEW: Corrosive Blast (cost 29/-) – A new uncommon damage dealer that ignores even magic immunity and is
irrecoverable. This is a very niche spell when you face the need to damage a sky drake or magic immune hero
via spells or really need to deal irrecoverable damage. Otherwise, stick to lightning bolt for better cost
effectiveness.
Chimeras (cost -/180, 4 upkeep) – Now moves 4 and is mountaineer, feels more aggressive and threatening as
a result and will likely be your staple summoning unit halfway through the game. Research cost is also
decreased a bit to 2000 (from 2140).
Blazing March (cost 45/-) – Moved from rare to uncommon so that chaos can get a global combat effect like
prayer and black prayer around the same time as those other 2 realms. The spell now also boosts thrown.
Research cost is also reduced to 2200 to make it consistent with being Uncommon spell.
Chaos Rare Spells
Mystic Surge (cost 25/-) – Moved to rare from previously uncommon, removes the buggy 'healing immunity',
and a bit more likely to grant positive effects, thus more powerful than in Caster of Magic. Research cost is
increased to 2400 (from previously 1280) to be consistent with its current status as rare spell.
Fire Storm (cost -/180) – Its attack strength is increased to 14 (from previously 12) and research cost is
decreased to 2600 (from 2800) but trade value is decreased.
Chaos Rift (cost -/200, 5 upkeep) – Attack strength from the enchantment reduced to 9 per strike (from
previously 11). In addition to current effects, new recruits from cursed city has a 10% chance of permanently
receiving 1 random warp creature effect (0 resistance, 1/3 armor, or ½ attack), effect is permanent and could not
be dispelled.
Chaos Spawn (cost -/303, 8 upkeep) – Research cost is decreased to 3000 (from previously 3200) but upkeep
cost is increased to 8 (from previously 5).
NEW: Chaos’ Blessing (cost -/200, 5 upkeep) – Rare level city enchantment that grants chaos channels to
recruited units and defending city has Warp Reality cast in combat. It has synergy with Doom Mastery (which
has been moved to very rare tier). Chaos’ Blessing also grants power to enchanted cities for each mountain (+1)
and volcano (+3) tiles in the vicinity. Chaos’ Blessing might give you an early advantage as not every city is a
unit producing center at that point and if defending primarily with chaos units, warp reality gives you a very
significant advantage.
Inner Power (cost -/600, 20 upkeep) – Now casting costs is increased significantly (from previously 390) and
slightly increase of trade value due to obvious combo with insulation. Also grants mountaineer to friendly units in
combat. Research cost is decreased to 3500 (from previously 3600).
NEW: Warp Lightning (cost 36/-) – Rare level combat spell that replacing old spell with same name that
hardcoded could not change. Warp Lightning hits all figures in a target unit with strength-9 (60% hit) lightning
damage, providing Chaos wizards and efreets and effective counter to multi-figure units.
Magic Vortex (cost 50/-) – I have struggled with idea of remove or replace this spell for very long time but in the
end I decide to just reduced its trade value instead.
Doom Bolt (cost 45/-) – Research cost is reduced to 4000 (from previously 4800) and trade value is reduced
slightly.
Doom Bat (cost -/300, 7 upkeep) – Now costs is reduced to 300 (from previously 320) and fiery immolation aura
of the original Master of Magic is coming back as well.
NEW: Blood and Iron (cost -/600, 25 upkeep) – New rare level global enchantment, bring chaos supremacist
war drum to your populance with cities of caster’s home race or integrate to Chaos realm with Chaos’s blessing
gain +30% production while other cities that alienated by this suffer +3 Unrest (which could be convert to 6
power by Chaos Embrace below). The same for regular units, regular units of the home race or with chaos
channel gains bonus while units that not fit racial criteria would suffer penalty instead.
NEW: Shatter (cost 20/-) – Rare level combat curse, Shatter has been revised to target any unit (not just normal
units) and with resistance penalty of -5. What makes this spell stand out is casting it with your magisters and
other caster units due to its low cost.
NEW: Beat of Swiftness (cost 55/-) – Rare level combat enchantment, all friendly units with melee>range gain
+3 movement, the rest get +2 movement. As a penalty, friendly units lose 10% of their armor. This spell further
enhances Chaos' strength at quick battle resolution and grants yet another offense advantage.
Efreet (cost -/333, 9 upkeep) – has caster 39 to prevent it from casting the new shatter twice.
Flame Strike (cost 60/-) – Damage scheming changes to strength 16 at 60% To-Hit on all units (from previously
strength 32 at 30% To-Hit). Research cost is also decreased to 5200 (from 5600).
Disintegrate (cost 50/-) – Moved down from very rare to rare tier with research cost of 5500 and reduces trade
value as this spell resistance threshold is not that justified to be very rare tier spell.
Warp Reality (cost 75/-) – Another spell that move down from very rare in Caster of Magic to rare tier in
Warlord. This spell used to be rare tier in original Master of Magic. Lack of doom mastery in rare tier indirectly
weakened this spell.
NEW: Incinerate (cost 55/-) – Hit target unit with strong fire attack (strength 18 Magical Fire attack at 60% To-
Hit + strength 18 Non-Magical Fire attack at 60% To-Hit) and then hit surrounding with non-magical fire attack
with half of the strength (18 Non-Magical Fire attack at 60% To-Hit) of at the center. More effective than Flame
Strike when hit enemy that cower behind the wall or stay in tight formation.
NEW: Fire Drake (cost -/390, 10 upkeep) – This spell could only be learned with Conjuring Pact and 6 Chaos
spell books.
Chaos Very Rare or Higher Spells
Doom Mastery (cost -/666, 18 upkeep) – Moved to very rare (Same as original Master of Magic) – grants all 3
effects if unit recruited in a city with 'chaos blessing' on them, or chaos channels cast on a hero, or new casting
attempt of Chaos Channels. Doom Mastery is also boosting Warp Creature spell by trigger all 3 effects instead
of just one. The stacking of chaos creature benefits got to be too excessive when considering other chaos spell
changes, but you no longer can rely on using such a strategy in every game (unless you pick 10 chaos books)
Hydra (cost -/480, 11 upkeep) – The creature gains more characteristic of Greek mythology; thus it now could
swim, breath changed to lightning breath, and high poison damage was also given. Unit also has lightning
resistance, thus benefits from inner power global enchantment, and can be an excellent offensive creature when
paired with the new 'Beat of Swiftness' spell. The research cost is reduced to 8000 (from previously 10000).
Chain Lightning (cost 65/-) – Attack power scheme changes to strength 20 at 60% To-Hit (from previously
strength 40 at 30% To-Hit), Research cost is decreased to 10000 (from previously 20000) due to this spell is that
far more superior than Incineration or Flame Strike to justified status as penultimate spell of research tree.
Chaos Surge (cost -/1000, 30 upkeep) – Given Doom Mastery, this spell is comparable to life realm's global
spells and even stacks, thus had to be made less accessible with research cost is increased to 12000 (from
previously 6000) to keep Chaos from being overpowered in large, crowded games.
Apocalypse (cost 65/-) – Research cost is decreased to 14000 (from previously 15000).
Great Drake (cost -/500, 15 upkeep) – The Great Drake is also given mountaineer, lightning resistance,
immolation, and cause fear for consistency (to match doom drakes).
Doomsday (cost -/1000, 20 upkeep) – Although trade value of the spell is decreased slightly due to the spell
does not deliver direct benefit toward the caster, the spell is more powerful with the effect of corruption that
randomly decay terrain toward less productive land even after corruption has been purified.
NEW: Dissolution (cost 80/-) – This new combat spell is a guaranteed 9 armor-piercing irrecoverable damage
(equivalent to 30 strength spell) per figure before shields. This spell's extraordinary power almost always wipes
out massively enchanted multi-figure units, thus acting as a counter against mega-buffing strategies.
Call the Void (cost -/500) – The spell is the same as what it ever was in Caster of Magic for Windows. It might
be slightly more powerful than previous version due to corruption’s terrain decay effect.
Blazing Eyes →Chaos Embrace (cost -/1300, 80 upkeep) – Blazing Eye is renamed to Chaos Embrace and
given a far higher casting cost (from previously 900) and research cost is increased to 20000 (from previously
8000), thus reducing the chance of stacking global effects to chaos units (see chaos surge above). This new
spell grants 2 power income for each of rebel population in caster’s cities. At the same time, each of rebel in the
city own by other wizards who not cast Chaos Embrace would deal 0.5 Doom damage to garrison of the city.
This would make the caster thrive as the world burned.
Meteor Storm (cost -/990, 10 upkeep) – Casting cost and trad value are slightly increased. Spell now also has
additional effect to give additional hit to the target when ever casting Fire Bolt, Fireball, or Fire Storm with
Magical Fire attack strength 75% of the original preceeding attack.
Armageddon (cost -/1250, 40 upkeep) – Now is considered the highest Chaos spell by research cost, but it is
slightly weaker than in Caster of Magic due to AI is more eager to disjunct it and damage to relationship with
other wizards is much more severe.
NEW: Chaos Mastery (reform, effect taken upon researched) – Increases enchantment dispel resistance,
reduces casting cost of the spells, and buff creature of the Chaos realm under wizard control. This reform is only
available to Specialist retort holder with Chaos as primary realm. Once this spell appears on research page, it
will exclude chance to get mastery of other realm.
NEW: Lesser Chaos Lord (cost -/777, 20 upkeep) – This spell could only be learned with Conjuring Pact and
10 Chaos spell books.
NEW: Great Chaos Lord (cost -/999, 30 upkeep) – This spell could only be learned with Conjuring Pact and 12
Chaos spell books.
NEW: Power of Chaos (cost 90/-) – This spell could only be learned by Enchanter wizard who already have
access to Fiery Fury, Immolation, Insulation, and Chaos Channels. This spell would allow the Enchanter to cast
all above unit enchantment all at once on single target!
NEW: Conduit of Chaos (cost 150/-) – This spell could only be learned by Runemaster wizard who already
have access to Breakthrough, Blazing March, Beat of Swiftness, and Warp Reality. This spell would allow the
Runemaster to cast all above combat enchantment all at once!
Life:
Life realm specializes in stacking enchantments on your recruitable units to a level where they can easily defeat
more advanced foes or defeat entire armies single-handed unscathed. Careful management of unit
enchantments on a turn-by-turn basis rewards the most detail-oriented players that can micromanage and keep
track of these buffs.
Given that the Warlord mod intends to keep normal units relevant throughout all stages of the game, this often
translates to unremarkable units being boosted individually to an unmatched level at the beginning or at the end
of a game. The importance of these units is addressed by giving life wizards tools to preserve such units or their
enchantments.
Cities can be viewed similarly in that they can individually perform far beyond other wizards with the help of city
enchantment stacking.
New spells further establish these realm characteristics.
Removed Life Spells
Discipline (cost -/-) – No longer researchable, but become Life ability that could be cast by Centurion hero and
can now also target heroes. The spell, stacked with herosim, broke the balance of very early game for wizards
with life books, resulting in units too strong against lairs and wizards before dispel magic is researched. The
enchantment is also grant to unit upon create if Enlightenment is casted (see below) and make the powerful
discipline+heroism combos more difficult to achieve at the beginning of the game.
Zeal (cost -/-) – used to castable in earlier version but now become Life ability that could be casted by Inquisitors
unit and Grand Inquisitor hero, grants first strike and negate first strike to unit until rest of combat.
Resurrection (cost -/325) – shifted to arcane rare with 3200 research cost.
Life Common Spells
Star Fires (cost 12/-) – One of the more efficient direct damage spell in term of cost with no elemental properties
but could only damage fantastic creature. Damage scheme is changed to strength 12 at 60% To-Hit (from
previously strength 23 at 30% To-Hit). But as it is now much less efficient than Fire Bolt, trade value is
decreased.
Guardian Spirit (cost -/60, 1 upkeep) – The creature has 1 less armor, but comes with healer, giving it a more
supportive role. Trade value of the spell is increased.
Holy Weapon (cost 8/40, 0 upkeep) – Research cost is decreased slightly to 240 (from previously 260) and
trade value is increased.
Bless (cost 7/35, 0 upkeep) – grants 4 resistance (-1 from original) and 7 armor (+2 from original) against
chaos/death effects as well as all attack with fire or lightning element. Research cost is decreased to 240 (from
previously 320).
Healing (cost 15/-) – Research cost is decreased to 280 (from 320).
Holy Armor (cost 10/50, 0 upkeep) – Research cost is decreased to 280 (from 320).
Heroism (cost 15/75, 1 upkeep) – Research cost is decreased to 280 (from 320).
NEW: True Light (cost 20/-) – Combat enchantment that grants +1 to all stats for life units, -1 to all stats for
death/undead units. True light also weakens illusion attacks by -10% to hit. Warlord mod restores a spell from
original Master of Magic, but has more synergy in mod thanks to uncommon spell sanctify. The minor extra
effect against illusion helps keep realm balanced after the loss of a major spell.
Heavenly Light (cost -/60, 1 upkeep) – Research cost is decreased to 400 (from previously 440) and trade
value is decreased significantly.
NEW: Spirit of Community (cost -/300, 9 upkeep) – Grants +4 production to all cities and doubles output
growth ideal for boosting growth of new towns, but not overly effective on well-developed cities. One of the best
spells to pick as 'starting common' for players that like to build up their empire peacefully. However, this spell can
also help out when conquering towns that had their production-generating structures destroyed in battle.
Life Uncommon Spells
True Sight (cost 12/60, 1 upkeep) – Casting cost is now lower (from previously 15/75) and also grants +5% to
range. Research cost is increased to 500 (from previously 420).
Exorcise (cost 18/-) – Casting cost is decreased (from previously 20/-) but research cost is increased to 700
(from previously 640).
Sanctify (cost -/60, 2 upkeep) – Spell gains additional effect with units also become life-realm non-fantastic units
during combat, helping protect against normal-unit oriented death spells. If cast on a 'cleric' unit (e.g. priest), it
turns unit into life fantastic creature during combat, grants +2 spellcasting skill per base resistance of unit. When
combine this with Pillar of Faith, some of cleric units would able to cast powerful life spell such as Prayer.
Just Cause (cost -/300, 5 upkeep) – The spell moves up tier to Uncommon (from previously Common) spell and
unrest reduction changes from -1 to -2. Spell gains additional effect of buffing hero and units within the same
stack as hero in combat.
Altar of Peace → Altar of Duality (cost -/100, 4 upkeep) – Grants either 12-32 research or 6-16 production
depending on how positive (or negative) wizard relations are. The spell was considered too weak as a
conditional 0-24 research spell that costs research to learn it and discouraged aggression, which is needed by
life to stay competitive. By gaining production when relations are negative, you can build up troops and
conquered towns with more ease.
Endurance (cost -/60, 2 upkeep) – Trade value is increased.
New: Divine Protection (cost 22/110, 1 upkeep) – New rare tier unit enchantment, giving a regular unit Lucky
(+10% To-Hit, +10% To-Defend, +1 Resistance) and Death Immunity. This cheaper counterpart of Lionheart is
based on Life realm item power of the same name. The spell cost is intentionally allow to be within castable
range of elite Magisters or sanctified cleric with base Resistance higher than 10.
Stream of Life (cost -/120, 4 upkeep) – Research cost is increased to 1400 (from previously 1280).
Unicorn (cost -/190, 4 upkeep) – The creature is now coming with Purify, helping clean corrupted land. Unicorn
also gains Forester.
Raise Dead (cost 40/-) – Research cost is decreased to 1800 (from previously 1920).
NEW: Hierophany (cost 23/-) – Combat curse with half resistance roll. If resistance roll unsuccessful, unit loses
half armor, all immunities, lightning resistance, negate first strike, and all mobility-related perks.
Prayer (cost 40/-) – Now grants +1 attack, armor and resistance when stacked with high prayer (to hit and to
defend do not stack). Research cost is increased to 2200 (from previously 2140).
NEW: Simurgh (cost -/140, 3 upkeep) – This spell could only be learned with Conjuring Pact and 4 Life spell
books.
Life Rare Spells
Prosperity (cost -/120, 2 upkeep) – The spell is retained its characteristic from Caster of Magic for Windows.
NEW: Inquisition (cost -/200, 4 upkeep) – Life gets 1 city curse, but not a traditional one. Inquisition penalizes
religious centers (for religious power beyond 6, each additional point reduces research by 3 and adds ½ unrest).
This city curse causes a minimum of 2 unrest, but unrest penalty will exceed it if religious power of cursed city
exceeds 10. Its high cost and effect on average towns disappoint, but with ideal targets it will eliminate all
research, weaken Uranus blessing, and punish Ruler of Heaven, Dark Ritual, by causing considerable unrest.
NEW: Heart of Solidarity (cost -/500, 15 upkeep) – Global Enchantment that eliminates unrest penalty from
racial relations and garrisons that are not full (morale treated as if full garrisons were in every town). It will help
boost taxes without harming your conquered cities, which suffer from racial unrest and small garrisons. The spell
is game changing when playing with or conquering klackons or goblins.
Exaltation (cost 25/-) – casting cost is decreased (from previously 30) while retained its healing effect. Research
cost is increased to 3000 (from previously 2800).
NEW: Angelic Guardians (cost -/500, 35 upkeep) – Global enchantment that in combat, it gives all normal units
under your command the ability to exorcise at -0, all life and sanctified units under your command the ability to
exorcise at -1, and if the unit already has exorcise ability, it gains added -2 strength (normal units) or added -3
strength (life unit). Note that undead units suffer -3 extra penalty, making this global enchantment extremely
dangerous for death wizards!
Mass Healing (cost 35/-) – Research cost is decreased to 3500 (from previously 4000).
Divine Order (cost -/600, 30 upkeep) – Originally underwhelming with the chance of backfiring in you. Cost
penalties of +25% for attack spells, unit and city curses apply only to enemy wizards. 25% cost bonuses apply to
buffs and healing spells. Additional 10% cost bonuses and penalties apply to global spells while summons cost
10% more. All cost increases affect opponents only so it would only limit opponent but caster still retain option to
continue their preferred strategy. Two additional small effects also introduced: +1unrest penalty and half power
income from magic markets to wizards with fewer life books than non-life books (+2 unrest and no magic market
bonus if wizard has no life books at all!). Due to spell becomes more powerful, trade value of this spell is
increased significantly.
Angel (cost -/310, 8 upkeep) – Spell and creature is more or less the same as it was in Caster of Magic for
Windows. The only difference is now summon artwork is more beautiful.
Invulnerability (cost 30/150, 5 upkeep) – The spell is the same as it was in Caster of Magic for Windows.
Lionheart (cost 36/180, 3 upkeep) – The spell is the same as it was in Caster of Magic for Windows.
NEW: Pillar of Faith (cost -/180, 5 upkeep) – City buff that gives 20% of granting lucky to recruited units and +1
to +8 Resistance depending on how many religious buildings you have in it. This allows wizard an opportunity to
gain a lucky unit to cast common tier buffs and addresses the loss of permanent discipline early in game. It also
generates 0.5 overland casting skill for each unrest reduction generates by religious buildings.
Altar of Battle (cost -/275, 5 upkeep) – Casting cost is decreased (from previously 300) and research cost is
decreased to 3800 (from previously 4400).
Inspirations (cost -/150, 4 upkeep) – Research cost is increased to 4600 (from 3200).
NEW: Valkyries (cost -/370, 9 upkeep) – A flying teleporting support unit with +2 resist to all, 2 charges of
exaltation, flying teleporting, and decent melee stats. A similar role as unicorn, but far superior.
Holy Word (cost 60/-) – Research cost is increased to 5200 (from previously 4800).
Incarnation (cost -/700, 15 upkeep) – Research cost is increased to 5500 (from previously 5200) and upkeep is
increased to 15 (from previously 12). The hero is no longer the “Chosen”, but now the “Avatar”.
Holy Arms (cost -/600, 10 upkeep) – Reserch cost is increased to 5800 (from previously 5600). The spell was
used to be Very Rare in original Master of Magic and Caster of Magic for DOS. The spell is moved down to rare
tier since Caster of Magic for Windows and this continues in Warlord mod.
New: Eye of Heaven (cost 60/-) – new rare tier Life realm combat enchantment, grants all friendly units True
Sight. The spell used to be only castable by Life creatures but now transfer to be castable by wizard instead.
Life Very Rare or Higher Spells
Consecration (cost -/200, 2 upkeep) – Enchanted city now produces bless to newly recruited units (only if
cathedral or temple exists in city). Research cost is increased to 8000 (from previously 6000)
Enlightenment (cost -/900, 50 upkeep) – the research bonus is reduced by half. However, newly produced units
now come with 'discipline'. This can be very useful when you have 'altar of battle' or 'crusade + warlord'. Upkeep
was increased to 50 to compensate for this powerful new effect, despite the halved research effect.
Phoenix (cost -/450, 12 upkeep) – this underwhelming creature was given some fire breath, immolation and
slightly higher defense stats. Research cost is decreased to 10000 (from previously 12000).
Destiny → Apotheosis (cost -/360, 10 upkeep) – Casting cost is decreased (from previously 400), and could
removes no-healing status from an undead unit. Trade value of the spell is increased slightly while research cost
is decreased to 12000 (from previously 15000).
Ruler of Heaven (cost -/1000, 25 upkeep) – Now adds 50 combat skill points for every religious power in your
cities, thus fully developed religious centers may gain about half of the effect of 'linking Towers' thanks to this
spell. Research cost is increased to 14000 (from previously 12000).
High Prayer (cost 70/-) – Now High Prayer’s and Prayer’s could stack but not at full effect (as discussed earlier).
Life Force (cost -/900, 40 upkeep) – The spell is retained its characteristic from Caster of Magic for Windows.
Supreme Light (cost 70/-) – Research cost is decreased to 16000 (from previously 18000).
Call to Arms → Spirit of Chivalry (cost 80/-) – It didn't feel 'awesome' for a very rare spell to summon an
already-existing normal unit. What this spell summons is a hero-like life unit with supportive effects and paladin-
like stats, albeit as a single-figure unit. It is overall superior to a 0-experience paladin, thus comes with a higher
cost (from previously 70). However, do not expect it to single-highhandedly win battles late in the game. It
remains a spell that boosts surrounding units and can be used as desperation if what you need is an additional
melee unit in play. Research cost is increased to 18000 (from previously 15000).
Crusade (cost -/1200, 20 upkeep) – Cities with armorer's guild + cathedral/temple grant holy armor to newly
produced unit. All those building requirements must be met for this added effect, so only some races can benefit
and only if you dedicate the time to construct these buildings. This can help reduce spell buff micromanagement
by providing holy armor to some units.
Arch Angel (cost -/600, 18 upkeep) – Now Arch Angel can cast hierophany in addition to caster 29, mostly for
flavor.
Charm of Life (cost -/1500, 30 upkeep) – Research cost is decreased to 22000 (from previously 24000).
NEW: Life Mastery (reform, effect taken upon researched) – Increases enchantment dispel resistance, reduces
casting cost of the spells, and buff creature of the Life realm under wizard control. This reform is only available to
Specialist retort holder with Life as primary realm. Once this spell appears on research page, it will exclude
chance to get mastery of other realm.
NEW: Seraph (cost -/999, 30 upkeep) – This spell could only be learned with Conjuring Pact and 12 Life spell
books.
NEW: Power of Life (cost 120/-) – This spell could only be learned by Enchanter wizard who already have
access to Bless, Heroism, Holy Armor, Holy Weapon, Endurance, Divine Protection, True Sight, Lionheart, and
Invulnerability. This spell would allow the Enchanter to cast all above unit enchantment all at once on single
target!
NEW: Day of Life (cost 150/-) – This spell could only be learned by Runemaster wizard who already have
access to True Light, Eye of Heaven, Prayer, High Prayer, and Supreme Light. This spell would allow the
Runemaster to cast all above combat enchantment all at once!
Death:
A heavily adjusted realm, given its underwhelming performance by players and opponent wizards.
More opportunities for raising undead were introduced throughout all stages of the game. Reliance on plentiful
and cheap undead armies, best amassed by defensive and calculating players, is a feature of Death. This helps
overwhelm the enemy with sheer numbers while building up your city garrison unit counts across the world at
little to no cost. Alongside your large armies of arguably weaker units you have various curse and debuff tools at
your disposal. Death gameplay is the opposite of life gameplay: it relies on weakening the enemy to win the
game, rather than strengthening itself. This theme applies to units, cities, and wizards themselves.
Death realm no longer associated with poison damage.
Note: Cult Leader now grants +100% power bonus from religious buildings, but dark rituals redesigned and
stacks less significantly.
Removed Death Spells
Final Wave – Now resistance roll of -1 (from 0), due to more opportunities to raise resistance in Warlord mod,
and top tier units innately having higher resistance.
Death Common Spells
Skeletons (cost -/25, 0 upkeep) – There is no change in spell and creature itself but ai has more incentive to
cast the spell.
Weakness (cost 8/-) – Casting cost is increased (from previously 7) and now the curse has no resistance roll.
The curse also has additional reduction of breath strength. This is now one of Death's staple common-tier curse
spells and worth picking as a starting common.
Cloak of Fear (cost 12/60, 1 upkeep) – Trade value is increased slightly while research cost is descreased to
240 (from 260).
Black Sleep (cost 15/-) – Trade value is decreased significantly due to it is only useful early and mid game.
Research cost is decreased to 240 (from previously 320).
Zombies (cost 24/-, 0 upkeep) – Received a 'resident evil update', now move 2 and have 5 base attack. These
are now a more reliable tool for raising undead (including with zombie mastery). These are also a higher threat
as rampaging monsters and lair defenders (their value increased). Casting cost is increased to 24 (from
previously 20) and research cost is decreased to 280 (from previously 320).
Life Drain (cost 10/-) – Research cost is decreased to 280 (from previously 320).
Ghouls (cost -/80, 1 upkeep) – Casting of the spell is lower (from previously 88). The unit get overhaul with
+10% to hit, but without poison. Death no longer involved in poison damage. Research cost is reduced to 320
(from previously 380).
Darkness (cost 20/-) – The spell is not changed from Caster of Magic for Windows.
Wraith Form (cost 11/55, 2 upkeep) – unchanged but weapon immunity now grants +10 armor and wraithform is
the only common-tier source of weapon immunity (fire elemental buffed and moved to uncommon-tier).
Research cost is decreased to 360 (from previously 440).
Misfortune → Liability (cost 13/-) – Research cost is decreased to 400 (from previously 480).
Death Uncommon Spells
Blood Lust → Bloodlust (cost 21/63, 0 upkeep) – Research is decreased to 500 (from previously 640) and
trade value is decreased. The spell is no longer grants the various immunities and enchanted units can heal
naturally (if enchanted overland). Blood Lust can be cast in combat for 21 cost. This is a great benefit for mono-
death wizards who lack tools to defeat blessed units and now you no longer have to deal with the consequences
of enchanted unit becoming undead. If cast on an appropriate melee unit next to a hero or other valuable normal
unit, it can turn the tide of battle.
Lycanthropy (cost -/95, 2 upkeep) – Werewolves gains Forester, +1 resistance, and Rage ability (+1 Attack
strength for each fallen figure in the unit), and cost 10 less (95 mana). Trade value of the spell is decreased but
research cost is increased to 700 (from previously 420). The cost of sacrificing a unit (spearmen more expensive
in mod), the higher research cost (700 from 420) led to lycanthropy being a disappointing spell. With small
bonuses and a lower cost, it should stay competitive.
Night Stalker (cost -/225, 1 upkeep) – Now the creature has stealth, because it is already invisible. Research
cost is decreased to 900 (from previously 1920).
Mana Leak (cost 20/-) – Research cost is decreased to 1000 (from previously 1280).
Syphon Life (cost 30/-) – Research cost is decreased to 1100 (from previously 1280).
New: Shadow Strike (cost 18/90, 2 upkeep) – This death uncommon unit enchantment, grant unit thrown attack
at strength 1/3 of melee strength. If thrown already a unit trait, then gain 1/3 of melee strength as additional
thrown damage. Ability to hit flyers is not a death realm trait, but this spell grants an opportunity to do so for your
ground military. While this all sounds underwhelming for the cost, please note that thrown is an additional attack,
therefore abilities like poison or life steal get to trigger twice while attacking!
Warp Node (cost -/120) – moved to uncommon-tier to grant death realm an economy boost spell in early to mid
game that is not overly powerful, but can harm opponents as a bonus. Trade value and research cost are
decreased to proportional to its current uncommon status.
Possession (cost 35/-) – Research cost is increased to 1400 (from previously 1280).
Black Prayer (cost 35/-) – Trade value is decreased significantly.
Wall of Darkness (cost 30/90, 1 upkeep) – Research cost is increased to 1800 (from previously 960) and trade
value is increased slightly.
Shadow Demons (cost -/175, 4 upkeep) – Research cost is decreased to 2000 (from previously 2140) and trade
value is decreased.
New: Revenant (cost 25/-) – New death uncommon combat unit enchantment, grant unit melee death touch 0
and regeneration 1 but unit permanently becomes undead. Note that death touch triggers once per attacking
figure, becoming devastating when using multi-figure melee units against lower resistance units. Death touch
does not apply to ranged attacks. This spell is also useful for preserving units you expect to die in combat while
enjoying the benefits of undead (added immunities, synergy with darkness).
NEW: Werewolves (cost 30/-, 2 upkeep) – Different from Lycanthropy, this spell is combat summon version.
This spell could only be learned with Conjuring Pact and 4 Death spell books.
Death Rare Spells
Drain Power (cost -/100) – Trade value is increased slightly.
Reaper Slash (cost 44/-) – The spell is now on rare-tier. The spell is damaging with cold undead-raising
damage, rather than poison. Strength increased to 22 (60% hit chance). Death no longer associated with poison
damage. Trade value is increased slightly and research cost adjusted to 2600 (from previously 1280) as it is now
rare tier spell.
Evil Presence (cost -/200, 3 upkeep) – Casting cost is increased (from previously 180) and trade value is
significantly increased. The spell does not only prevent units from being recruited with experience or magic
weapons, but now also prevents positive recruitment effects introduced by warlord mod, such as effects from
Survival Instinct, free disciplines/resist elements, doom mastery, etc
Drought (cost -/200, 3 upkeep) – Casting cost is increased (from previously 150) as now the spell also reduces
city food production by 25% and newly recruited units, malnourished, are debuffed with 1 less melee and 2 less
armor. Trade value is decreased slightly and research cost is decreased to 3000 (from previously 3200).
Wraiths (cost -/250, 5 upkeep) – Casting cost is cheaper (from previously 350) and research cost decreased
significantly to 3200 (from previously 4800). But this comes with weaker stats, particularly in the melee
compartment. This may increase the chances (with black prayer) to raising undead. Earlier versions of mod has
guaranteed raise undead, but the ability was instead given to Vampire (more thematic). Trade value is
decreased slightly as result.
Dark Rituals (cost -/150, 0 upkeep) – Now grants 8 base power + 100% of religious power (instead of 0 +200%
religious power) due to major stacking imbalances around other mod changes. Research cost is decreased to
3500 (from previously 4000).
Terror (cost 40/-) – Research cost is decreased to 3800 (from 4000).
Fate Mastery → Dance of Death (cost -/444, 17 upkeep) – The spell is moved from Chaos realm to Death
realm due to it fits better under death, can help boost some of the curse combat spells. Moved to rare tier for
better progression on resistance-reducing effects. Research cost is increased to 4000 to match its current status
as rare tier spell. Trade value is also increased significantly due to how important the spell is for Death realm
playstyle.
NEW: State of Rot (cost -/600, 30 upkeep) – New global enchantment, all enemy non-undead units in combat
lose regeneration, cannot heal in combat. Additionally, your undead units outside of combat heal by 3hp per
turn.
Gate of Hades (cost 40/-) – The spell does not change from Caster of Magic for Windows.
NEW: Arch Liches (cost -/360, 8 upkeep) – New Death rare tier summon creature. These dark priests of the
Death are combination of priest, magisters, and ghouls with ability to cast death realm spells, grant Resistance
for all, deal long range attack with life steal, and summon a lot of zombie to aid the combat. This creature is a
great aid to death realm that overall suffer from low resistance.
Vampire → Vampire Lord (cost -/395, 10 upkeep) – Slightly name change to make them classier and match
with another newly added spell in term of theme. The creature now has Lower hp, regeneration, and melee
output. However, it now has higher resistance and comes with a free charge of syphon life to assist with self-
healing and undead creation and the vampire is guaranteed to raise undead via melee damage. Trade value is
increased to match its new additional role as main undead creator and research cost is decreased to 4300 (from
previously 4400).
NEW: Soul Flay (cost 45/-) – Combat irresistible curse to normal units or heroes that reduces 1 melee, 2 armor
and 2 resistance for each experience level (-2 recruit, -8 elite for armor and resistance). This spell can be
devastating for heroes that leveled up 5+ times and ultra-elite or champion units, most commonly seen from life
wizards. This spell now establishes itself as the ultimate anti-hero tool, taking the place of 'crack's call'
Wave of Despair (cost 72/-) – Trade value is decreased significantly and research cost is decreased to 4900
New: Vampirism (cost -/100, 3 upkeep) – New Death very rare overland unit enchantment, normal unit
becomes undead, cannot gain experience (but heroism still able to buff them), creates undead, gains
bloodsucker, and has all thrown/breath transferred to melee and reduced thrown/breath strength to 1 (so it still
able to attack air). Note that enchanted unit cannot gain experience so keep this drawback in mind when casting
this spell on heroes. The thrown/breath shift to melee was done to reduce abusable double-triggering of blood
sucker.
Summon Demon (cost 50/150, 3 upkeep) – A slightly name changes and move down the spell from very rare to
now a rare-tier spell. Casting cost is increased to 50 (from previously 41) to prevent positive return of casting skill
by summoning them in combat. Demon also comes with slightly increased stats and the ability to raise undead
via melee damage. It is also a more expensive spell. It is difficult for it to win battles with mediocre melee stats,
thus proven not to be game breaking. The most reliable raise-undead feature from the original unit (caster 40,
thus 4 life drains or syphon life) remains. This is also an indirect enhancement to Demon Lord. Research cost is
decreased to 5500 (from previously 6000) but research priority is significantly higher.
Zombie mastery (cost -/800, 40 upkeep) – This global enchantment (now more costly to maintain) grants +1 to
stats, including movement, to zombies and undead units to further enhance your undead-raising gameplay.
Research cost is increased to 5800 (from previously 5600) and trade value is increased significantly as result.
NEW: Necropolis (cost -/200, 4 upkeep) – New rare tier economic-oriented city enchantment for Death realm,
turn city of the livings into city of the deads binding to the wizard's will. Population units no longer affect by
Unrest and no longer Growth or Shrinkage normally. All newly trained units from the city become Undead. In
combat, Necropolis is protected by Gate of Hades combat enchantment.
NEW: Ghost Ship (cost -/220, 4 upkeep) – This spell could only be learned with Conjuring Pact and 6 Death
spell books.
Death Very Rare or Higher Spells
Animate Dead (cost 50/-) – Research cost is decreased significantly to 8000 (from previously 15000).
Ruler of Underworld (cost -/1300, 50 upkeep) – Research cost is decreased to 8000 (from previously 10000).
The spell now grants +4 religious power for each oracle in play (consults the dead), helping pay upkeep and
allowing minor combos with cult leader and ruler of heaven. Additionally, mod mechanics make it more usable
(weapon immunity boosted to +10 effect, more relevance of top-tier melee normal units)
Cloud of Shadow (cost -/250, 5 upkeep) – The spell is move up tier to very rare from previously rare tier. Its
trade value increased significantly along with casting costs increased (from previously 200). Research cost and
trade value increased significantly to match up with its current status as very rare spell.
Death Knights (cost -/420, 8 upkeep) – The creature get 1 spell charge of Cloak of Fear. Trade value is slightly
decreased.
Massacre (cost 60/-) – Research cost is decreased to 14000 (from previously 15000).
Annihilate (cost 41/-) – The spell has not changed from Caster of Magic for Windows.
Pestilence (cost -/250, 5 upkeep) – The city enchantment was powerful in theory, but difficult to properly use,
invalidating the claim that it 'wins the game'. The population killing rate of this spell has been increased
substantially, making it the ultimate economy-killing spell in the game. The spell has also gain new use as
combat debuff as garrison would suffer plague debuff in combat. Research cost increase (from 8000 to 15000)
was necessary to delay its introduction and require significant investments given the impact it has on the game.
Darkest Hour (cost -/1200, 40 upkeep) – the underwhelming global enchantment now comes with 3 unrest to all
opponent cities (and can stack with +2 when multiple versions in play), adding to the negative economy impact.
Wizard who casts darkest hour is immune to other wizards' darkest hour unrest effect. Research cost is
increased to 16000 (from previously 15000).
Eternal Night (cost -/1000, 24 upkeep) – In addition to the original effects, now makes all enemy non-death
units lose 2 range (poor sight) during combat as long as spell is in effect. Trade value and casting cost are
increased (from 800) as result.
Death Reckoning (cost -/1000, 30 upkeep) –
Evil Omens (cost -/1250, 25 upkeep) – now second or later copies give additional 25% casting cost and effect
could be prevented by own a copy of Evil Omens.
Demon Lord (cost -/666, 18 upkeep) – Research cost is decreased to 22000 (from previously 24000).
NEW: Death Mastery (reform, effect taken upon researched) – Increases enchantment dispel resistance,
reduces casting cost of the spells, and buff creature of the Death realm under wizard control. This reform is only
available to Specialist retort holder with Death as primary realm. Once this spell appears on research page, it will
exclude chance to get mastery of other realm.
NEW: Arch Demon Lord (cost -/999, 30 upkeep) – This spell could only be learned with Conjuring Pact and 12
Death spell books.
NEW: Power of Death (cost 150/-) – This spell could only be learned by Enchanter wizard who already have
access to Cloak of Fear, Wraith Form, Bloodlust, Shadow Strike, Revenant, and Vampirism. This spell would
allow the Enchanter to cast all above unit enchantment all at once on single target!
NEW: Night of Death (cost 150/-) – This spell could only be learned by Runemaster wizard who already have
access to Darkness, Mana Leak, Black Prayer, Terror, and Gate of Hades. This spell would allow the
Runemaster to cast all above combat enchantment all at once!
Other Gameplay Changes
Overland global spells cost more in games with higher # of opponents and larger land size than average.
Overland spells that are individual-based or localized cost slightly less in games with higher # of opponents and
larger land size.
Spell text now includes pictures that represents such spells.
Road and city tiles cost 0.5 movement point, but are more difficult to build.
AI wizards have altered decision-making, particularly when it comes to rush-buying buildings. They are now
discouraged (rather than strongly encouraged) to rush-buy wizard guild, amplifying tower, linking tower.
Combat terrain in forest and nature node has 55% rough terrain (from 95% and 35%, respectively) while
mountain and chaos node has 35% of rough terrain (from 8%).
Weapon immunity now grants +10 armor against non-magic weapons.
- First turn one could obtain 'rare' or 'very rare' spell in treasure much earlier.
It is more common to earn gold and mana rewards from lairs and less common to earn weak artifacts.
Advanced rewards such as high-tier spells, picks, vials, and hero prisoners require a higher minimum reward
treshhold, but only consumes a portion of this minimum, allowing space for other rewards (e.g. gold, mana,
items)
Neutral-only unit additions, such as the return of manticores, storm giants, sprites and a new 'ghost ship'.
Manticores no longer have weapon immunity.
Unit mercenaries can be hired as early as turn 18 (from 30), helping out wizards with benefactor (aka. famous)
and charismatic retorts. Items and heroes still show up no earlier than turn 30.
Aether Flux cost reduction effect weakened from 50% reduction to 33% reduction.
Good/Bad Moon religion power effect weakened, from -50% and +100% effects to -33% and +50% effects.
Rampage-only Lord Units
Lesser Chaos/Gaia/Aether Lords will begin showing up as rampaging monsters if game goes for too long. -
Lesser Lords are boss-type monsters that combine many traits of their respective realms and can single-
handedly defeat unprepared armies – these show up around final Spell of Mastery stage of the game.
-The greater lords (and a Seraph and an Arch Demon Lord) show up even later with greater stats, spellcasting
abilities and realm traits.
Experience Level Bonuses
+1 mp for each level of experience
Ultra Elite: +5% to hit, +1 attack, +1thrown/breath +1 armor, +1mp
(from the underwhelming +1 attack, +1 armor)
Champion: +5% to hit, +1 attack, +2 armor, +1 resistance, +1mp
(more balanced set of boosts instead of just +10% to hit, +1hp)
Endgame
Although the mod has no set time limit about how long game would drag long but there are a few factors that
would limit how long you could keep playing in single playthrough.
1) Rampaging Monsters
Rampaging monster will become more and more powerful as game continue and at some point monster
would become too powerful to deal with any place and anywhere. This could be lessen by clear out
monster lairs that kept spawning monsters but presence of Nature Embrace make the stream of
monsters go on. If your wizard does not have Nature Embrace, those monsters would overwhelm you at
some point of the game as Lords class monsters coming along with monster rampaging stack. In
advanced difficulty, this could occur around year 1525 (turn 300 onward) and this could occur in year
1513 (turn 150 onward) in highest difficulty like Phantasm.No. Total Budget multiplier start (1502/4) year 1505 year 1510 year 1515 year 1520 year 1525 year 1530

2) Spell of Mastery
Spell of Mastery is equivalent to scientific victory of other Civilization clone game. It is ultimate goal of
every wizards and all wizards who already have this spell would cast it sooner or later. Once the Spell of
Mastery coming into play, game reach its last phase once any wizard finished this spell, the game end
with that wizard’s victory and could not continue any further.
Change Logs:
Version 1.5.12.5
Spells:
• Great Unbinding is now working against lair monsters.
• Divine Judgement casting cost is now scale by land size and game scale setting.
• Spells those unlock by requirement will get spell on research page once requirement fulfilled.
• All new summons that only accessible by Conjurer are now gained custom priority.
• Rally gains casting priority and autocombat bonus.
• Whispering Echo gains casting priority and autocombat bonus.
• Divine Judgementg gains casting priority.
• Tabula Rasa gains casting priority and autocombat bonus.
• Force of Nature gains casting priority.
• Mystery of Sorcery gains casting priority.
• Conduit of Chaos gains casting priority.
• Day of Life gains casting priority.
• Night of Death gains casting priority.
• Custom priority of spell “Power of….” are increased.
Units:
• BUG FIX: Wanderer hero summons by Pandora Box ability.
• New hero ability: Righteous Ward, hero gains free permanent enchantments (mostly Life realm
enchantments) as hero level increases.
• New hero ability: Arcane Ward, hero gains free permanent enchantments (mostly Sorcery and Nature
realm enchantments) as hero level increases.
• New hero ability: Chaos Boon, hero gains more Chaos enchantments and abilities as hero level
increases.
• New hero ability: Death Ascension, hero gains more Death enchantments and abilities as hero level
increases.
• Wanderer hero gains additional abilities if wizard recruit her through Summon Champion or random
hiring offer.
• Wanderer hero under wizard with Channeler retort have spell charge change to combat summon if
wizard has Conjurer retort.
• Unit description of summonable creature would tell how many books requires for Conjurer to learn the
spell through Conjuring Pact spell.
• Javelineers’ Armor reduces from 3 to 2, gains Large Shield and has new sprites.
• New sprites for Lizardman Marines.
• New sprites for Lizardman Dragon Turtle.
• New sprites for Lizardman Shieldbearers.
• Jungle Stalkers’ Ranged Attack strength increases from 2 to 4, Armor from 3 to 4, Figure reduces from 4
to 2, cost reduces from 70 to 60, and Upkeep increases from 1 to 2.
• Cloud Elephant gains flag to be target of Focus Magic.
• Heroes’ Chosen of…. abilities are now restrict to heroes of unrestricted class.
• The Dervish hero class changes from Warrior to Warrior/Leader.
• The Ranger hero class changes from Unspecialized to Warrior/Mage.
• The Arcane Archer hero class changes from Unspecialized to Warrior/Mage.
• The Swarm Queen hero class changes from Unspecialized to Warrior/Leader.
• The King of the Deep hero clas changes from Unspecialized to Warrior/Leader.
• The Bronze Sentinel hero class changes from Unspecialized to Warrior/Mage and gains Arcane Ward
ability.
• The Avatar hero class changes from Unspecialized to Warrior/Leader, gains super Righteous Ward but
loses 2 random abilities.
• The Paladin hero gains Righteous Ward but super Might reduces to normal Might.

Others
• Score modifier rules now are organized and group based on type of modifiers…..
◦ Rules apply to everyone with little to no change in difficulty
◦ Rules of starting position
◦ Rules for quality of life and beginner player
◦ Rules that make game easier for human player
◦ Rules that drastically change gameplay
◦ Rules for skilled player who looking for challenge
• New score modifier “Book Collectors”, Each time a wizard is banished or defeated, there is a chance
that one of their spell books will become the winner's possession. The book will then no longer be
legible as far as its previous content is concerned, but it keeps all the other advantages, score modifier
= 0.75. Thanks Slingers and More Stuff mod for script content.
• New score modifier “Unstoppable Stampede”, In combat, all neutral fantastic creatures gain
regeneration 0, score modifier = 1.25. Thanks Slingers and More Stuff mod for inspiration.
• New score modifier “Adamantium Fortress”, Player wizard start with old adamantium mine right below
his fortress and his starting units equipped with adamantium equipments left over from previous owner,
score modifier = 0.6. Thanks Slingers and More Stuff mod for inspiration.
• New score modifier “Nodeborne Souls”, nodes will be more active in defending itself in combat by
randomly gives unit enchantment from the same realm as node on all defending neutral creatures and
randomly cast combat enchantment of the same realm before combat, score modifier = 1.5.
• New score modifier “Uphill Battle”, whenever AI units are in combat against human player, those units
gains +10% To-Hit, +10% To-Defend, and +1 Resistance, score modifier = 1.5.
• New score modifier “Gods Play Dices”, at the beginning of combat, each units roll for resistance
penalties (1% for -5, 2% for -4, 4% for -3, 8% for -2, and 16% for -1). Non-human players' units also
rolls for resistance penalties but only at half chance for each penalty level against the human player,
score modifier = 1.5.
• New score modifier “Khan the Conqueror”, neutral units will fight as if their commander have Warlord
and Tactician retorts, score modifier = 1.5.
• Frozen and Volcanic climate now triple spawn chance for wildgames on tundra tiles.
